# <a name="hololens-2-release-notes"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-103">HoloLens 2发行说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-103">HoloLens 2 release notes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-104">为了确保你在 HoloLens 设备上获得高效体验，我们将继续发布功能、bug 和安全更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-104">To ensure you have a productive experience with your HoloLens devices, we continue to release feature, bug, and security updates.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-105">在此页上，可以看到 HoloLens 每月的新增功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-105">On this page, you can see what’s new for HoloLens each month.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-106">若要获取最新的HoloLens 2更新，可以检查更新并手动更新，[](hololens-update-hololens.md#check-for-updates-and-manually-update)或获取完整闪存更新 (FFU) 通过高级恢复助手 来刷用[设备](hololens-recovery.md#clean-reflash-the-device)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-106">To get the latest HoloLens 2 update, you can either [check for updates and manually update](hololens-update-hololens.md#check-for-updates-and-manually-update) or get the Full Flash Update (FFU) to [flash your device via Advanced Recovery Companion](hololens-recovery.md#clean-reflash-the-device).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-107">[下载](https://aka.ms/hololens2download)会保持最新，并提供最新的已发布版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-107">The [download](https://aka.ms/hololens2download) is kept up to date and provides the latest generally available build.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-21h1"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-108">Windows Holographic 版本 21H1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-108">Windows Holographic, version 21H1</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-109">内部版本 20346.1002</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-109">Build 20346.1002</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-110">此更新包含两个目标受众的功能;最终用户可在设备上由任何人使用的功能，以及 IT 管理员可配置的新设备管理选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-110">This update contains features for two target audiences; features that can be used by anyone on a device by the End User, and new device management options that can be configured by IT Admins.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-111">下表指定与每个受众相关的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-111">The table below specifies the features that are relevant to each audience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-112">如果你是 IT 管理员，请查看我们的 IT 管理员 [- 更新清单](#it-admin---update-checklist)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-112">If you are an IT Admin, please take a look at our [IT Admin - Update Checklist](#it-admin---update-checklist).</span></span>
>[!IMPORTANT]
><span data-ttu-id="c256e-113">若要更新到此内部版本，HoloLens 2 设备 () 当前必须运行 2021 年 2 月更新 (内部版本 19041.1136) 或更高版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-113">In order to update to this build, HoloLens 2 device(s) must be currently running the February 2021 update (build 19041.1136) or newer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-114">如果看不到此功能更新可用，请先更新设备，然后重试。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-114">If you are not seeing this feature update available, please update your device first and try again.</span></span>

>[!NOTE]
><span data-ttu-id="c256e-115">目前，Microsoft HoloLens 2 支持每月服务更新 (bug 和安全修复) 适用于以下版本：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-115">Today, Microsoft HoloLens 2 supports monthly servicing updates (bug and security fixes) for the following releases:</span></span>
>- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-116">Windows Holographic 版本 20H2 (内部版本 19041.1128+) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-116">Windows Holographic, version 20H2 (Build 19041.1128+)</span></span>
>- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-117">Windows Holographic 版本 2004 (内部版本 19041.1103+) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-117">Windows Holographic, version 2004 (Build 19041.1103+)</span></span>
>- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-118">Windows Holographic 版本 1903 (内部版本 18362+) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-118">Windows Holographic, version 1903 (Build 18362+)</span></span> 
>
> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-119">随着 Windows Holographic 版本 21H1 的引入，我们将停止为 Windows 全息版本 **1903** 提供每月服务更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-119">With the introduction of Windows Holographic version 21H1, **we are discontinuing monthly servicing updates for Windows Holographic version 1903**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-120">这使我们能够专注于较新版本，并继续提供有价值的改进。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-120">This enables us to focus on more recent releases and continue to deliver valuable improvements.</span></span>

### <a name="introducing-the-new-microsoft-edge"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-185">推出新的 Microsoft Edge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-185">Introducing the new Microsoft Edge</span></span>

![将旧版 Microsoft Edge 徽标动画用于新的 Microsoft Edge 徽标](images/new-edge.gif)

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-187">新的 Microsoft Edge [采用 Chromium 开源项目](https://blogs.windows.com/windowsexperience/2018/12/06/microsoft-edge-making-the-web-better-through-more-open-source-collaboration/) ，为客户提供更好的兼容性，并为 web 开发人员创建更少的网络碎片。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-187">The new Microsoft Edge [adopts the Chromium open source project](https://blogs.windows.com/windowsexperience/2018/12/06/microsoft-edge-making-the-web-better-through-more-open-source-collaboration/) to create better compatibility for customers and less fragmentation of the web for web developers.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-188">这一新的 Microsoft Edge 会自动替换旧的 Microsoft Edge，新版本中 [不再支持](https://blogs.windows.com/msedgedev/2021/03/09/microsoft-edge-legacy-end-of-support/) 该版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-188">This new Microsoft Edge automatically replaces legacy Microsoft Edge, which is [no longer supported](https://blogs.windows.com/msedgedev/2021/03/09/microsoft-edge-legacy-end-of-support/) in new releases.</span></span>

![新的 Microsoft Edge 屏幕截图](images/new-edge-ui.png)

#### <a name="launching-the-new-microsoft-edge"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-190">启动新的 Microsoft Edge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-190">Launching the new Microsoft Edge</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-191">新的 Microsoft Edge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-191">The new Microsoft Edge</span></span> ![新的 Microsoft Edge 图标](images/new_edge_logo.png) <span data-ttu-id="c256e-193">用蓝色和绿色的漩涡图标表示的 () 固定到 "开始" 菜单，当你激活 web 链接时，将自动启动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-193">(represented by a blue and green swirl icon) is pinned to the Start menu and will automatically launch when you activate a web link.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-194">首次在 HoloLens 2 上启动新的 Microsoft Edge 时，将从旧的 Microsoft Edge 导入设置和数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-194">When you first launch the new Microsoft Edge on HoloLens 2, your settings and data will be imported from legacy Microsoft Edge.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-195">如果在启动新的 Microsoft Edge 后继续使用旧的 Microsoft Edge，则不会将新数据从旧的 Microsoft Edge 同步到新的 Microsoft Edge。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-195">If you continue to use legacy Microsoft Edge after launching the new Microsoft Edge, that new data will not be synced from legacy Microsoft Edge to the new Microsoft Edge.</span></span>

#### <a name="configuring-policy-settings-for-the-new-microsoft-edge"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-196">为新的 Microsoft Edge 配置策略设置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-196">Configuring policy settings for the new Microsoft Edge</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-197">新的 Microsoft Edge 为 IT 管理员提供了一组在 HoloLens 2 上提供的更广泛的浏览器策略，比以前在旧式 Microsoft Edge 中提供的更广泛。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-197">The new Microsoft Edge offers IT admins a much broader set of browser policies on HoloLens 2 than were previously available with legacy Microsoft Edge.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-198">下面是一些有用的资源，用于了解有关管理新的 Microsoft Edge 的策略设置的详细信息：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-198">Here are some helpful resources for learning more about managing policy settings for the new Microsoft Edge:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="c256e-199">配置 Microsoft Intune 的 Microsoft Edge 策略设置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-199">Configure Microsoft Edge policy settings with Microsoft Intune</span></span>](https://docs.microsoft.com/deployedge/configure-edge-with-intune)
- [<span data-ttu-id="c256e-200">Microsoft Edge 传统到 Microsoft Edge 策略映射</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-200">Microsoft Edge Legacy to Microsoft Edge policy mapping</span></span>](https://docs.microsoft.com/deployedge/microsoft-edge-policy-map-legacy-to-newedge)
- [<span data-ttu-id="c256e-201">Google Chrome 到 Microsoft Edge 策略映射</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-201">Google Chrome to Microsoft Edge policy mapping</span></span>](https://docs.microsoft.com/deployedge/microsoft-edge-policy-map-chrome-to-newedge)
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-202">完整的 [Microsoft Edge 企业文档](https://docs.microsoft.com/deployedge/)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-202">Full [Microsoft Edge Enterprise documentation](https://docs.microsoft.com/deployedge/)</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-203">由于新的 Microsoft Edge 支持浏览器策略的数量，我们的团队无法保证每个新策略都在 HoloLens 2 上运行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-203">Because of the volume of browser policies supported by the new Microsoft Edge, our team is unable to guarantee that each new policy works on HoloLens 2.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-204">但是，我们已测试并确认了与以前在 HoloLens 2 上所支持的每个旧版 Microsoft Edge 策略等效的新的 Microsoft Edge。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-204">However, we've tested and confirmed than the new Microsoft Edge equivalent of each legacy Microsoft Edge policy previously supported on HoloLens 2 work as expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-205">请参阅 [Microsoft Edge 旧版与 Microsoft edge 策略映射](https://docs.microsoft.com/deployedge/microsoft-edge-policy-map-legacy-to-newedge) ，查找与在 HoloLens 2 中使用的每个旧版 microsoft edge 浏览器策略等效的新的 microsoft edge。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-205">See [Microsoft Edge Legacy to Microsoft Edge policy mapping](https://docs.microsoft.com/deployedge/microsoft-edge-policy-map-legacy-to-newedge) to find the new Microsoft Edge equivalent of each legacy Microsoft Edge browser policy you were using with HoloLens 2.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-206">我们知道至少有两个新的Microsoft Edge策略 *将不能* 与HoloLens 2：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-206">There are at least two new Microsoft Edge policies that we know *will not* work with HoloLens 2:</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="c256e-207">EnterpriseModeSiteList</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-207">EnterpriseModeSiteList</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="c256e-208">EnterpriseSiteListServiceURL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-208">EnterpriseSiteListServiceURL</span></span>

#### <a name="what-to-expect-from-the-new-microsoft-edge-on-hololens-2"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-209">HoloLens 2 上新Microsoft Edge预期HoloLens 2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-209">What to expect from the new Microsoft Edge on HoloLens 2</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-210">由于新Microsoft Edge是一个本机 Win32 应用，具有新的 UWP 适配器层，允许它在 HoloLens 2 等仅 UWP 设备上运行，因此某些功能可能不会立即可用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-210">Because the new Microsoft Edge is a native Win32 app with a new UWP adapter layer allowing it to run on UWP-only devices like HoloLens 2, some features may not be immediately available.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-211">我们将支持未来几个月的新方案和功能，因此请查看此空间了解最新信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-211">We'll be supporting new scenarios and features over the coming months, so check this space for up-to-date information.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-212">**方案和功能预期可正常工作：**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-212">**Scenarios and features expected to work:**</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-213">首次运行体验、登录到配置文件和同步</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-213">First-run experience, sign in to profile, and sync</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-214">网站应按预期呈现和行为</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-214">Websites should render and behave as expected</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-215">大多数浏览器功能 (收藏夹、历史记录等) 应正常工作</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-215">Most browser functionality (Favorites, History, etc.) should work as expected</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-216">深色模式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-216">Dark mode</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-217">将 Web 应用安装到设备</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-217">Installing web apps to the device</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-218">安装扩展 (请使用任何无法正常使用扩展的扩展，请HoloLens 2) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-218">Installing extensions (please let us know if you use any extensions that don't work properly on HoloLens 2)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-219">查看和标记 PDF</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-219">Viewing and marking up a PDF</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-220">单个浏览器窗口中的空间声音</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-220">Spatial sound from a single browser window</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-221">自动和手动更新浏览器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-221">Automatic and manual updating of the browser</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-222">使用"保存到 PDF"选项 (从"打印"菜单保存 PDF) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-222">Saving a PDF from the Print menu (using "Save to PDF" option)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-223">WebXR 和 360 查看器扩展</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-223">WebXR and 360 Viewer extension</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-224">在环境中跨多个窗口浏览时，内容还原到正确的窗口</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-224">Content restoration to correct window, when browsing across multiple windows placed in your environment</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-225">**不应正常工作的方案和功能：**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-225">**Scenarios and features not expected to work:**</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-226">来自具有同步音频流的多个窗口的空间声音</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-226">Spatial sound from multiple windows with simultaneous audio streams</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-227">"看看它，说吧"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-227">"See it, say it"</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-228">打印</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-228">Printing</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-229">**最常见的浏览器已知问题：**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-229">**Top browser known issues:**</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-230">为新的 Microsoft Edge 禁用了全息键盘中的放大镜预览。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-230">The magnifier preview in the holographic keyboard has been disabled for the new Microsoft Edge.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-231">我们希望在未来的更新中重新启用此功能，一旦放大倍数工作正常。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-231">We hope to reenable this feature in a future update, once the magnification is working correctly.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-232">如果有另一个浏览器窗口处于打开和活动状态，则可以从错误的浏览器窗口播放音频。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-232">Audio may play from the wrong browser window if you have another browser window open and active.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-233">通过关闭不应播放音频的其他活动窗口，可以解决此问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-233">You can work around this issue by closing the other active window that isn't supposed to be playing audio.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-234">在 ["关注我" 模式下](hololens2-basic-usage.md#follow-me-stop-following)从浏览器窗口播放音频时，如果禁用 "关注我" 模式，则音频将继续播放。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-234">When playing audio from a browser window in ["Follow me" mode](hololens2-basic-usage.md#follow-me-stop-following), the audio will continue playing if you disable "Follow me" mode.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-235">可以通过在禁用 "关注我" 模式之前停止音频播放，或通过使用 **X** 按钮关闭窗口，来解决此问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-235">You can work around this issue by stopping audio playback before disabling "Follow me" mode or by closing the window with the **X** button.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-236">与活动 Microsoft Edge windows 交互可能会导致其他2D 应用程序窗口意外停用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-236">Interacting with active Microsoft Edge windows may cause other 2D app windows to go inactive unexpectedly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-237">您可以重新激活这些窗口，方法是再次与它们进行交互。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-237">You can reactivate these windows by interacting with them again.</span></span>

#### <a name="microsoft-edge-insider-channels"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-238">Microsoft Edge 预览体验渠道</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-238">Microsoft Edge Insider channels</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-239">Microsoft Edge 团队向边缘有问必答社区提供三个预览频道： Beta 版、开发人员版和 "未之限"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-239">The Microsoft Edge team makes three preview channels available to the Edge Insider community: Beta, Dev, and Canary.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-240">安装预览频道不会卸载 HoloLens 2 上的 Microsoft Edge 的发行版，并且可以同时安装多个版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-240">Installing a preview channel doesn't uninstall the released version of Microsoft Edge on your HoloLens 2, and you can install more than one at the same time.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-241">若要深入了解边缘有问必答社区，请访问 [Microsoft Edge 有问必答主页](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-241">Visit the [Microsoft Edge Insider homepage](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com) to learn more about the Edge Insider community.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-242">若要详细了解不同的边缘有问必答通道并开始，请访问 [边缘有问必答下载页面](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com/download)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-242">To learn more about the different Edge Insider channels and get started, visit the [Edge Insider download page](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com/download).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-243">有几种方法可用于将 Microsoft Edge 有问必答通道安装到 HoloLens 2：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-243">There are a couple methods available for installing Microsoft Edge Insider channels to HoloLens 2:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-244">**直接安装在设备上 (当前仅适用于非托管设备)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-244">**Direct install on device (currently only available to unmanaged devices)**</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-245">在 HoloLens 2 上，请访问 [边缘有问必答下载页面](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com/download)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-245">On your HoloLens 2, visit the [Edge Insider download page](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com/download).</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-246">选择要安装的边缘有问必答频道的 "下载" " **HoloLens 2** " 按钮。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-246">Select the **Download for HoloLens 2** button for the Edge Insider channel you wish to install.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-247">使用文件资源管理器) ，从边缘下载队列或设备的 "下载" 文件夹启动下载的 .msix 文件 (。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-247">Launch the downloaded .msix file from the Edge download queue or from your device's "Downloads" folder (using File Explorer).</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-248">将启动[应用安装程序](app-deploy-app-installer.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-248">[App installer](app-deploy-app-installer.md) will launch.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-249">选择“安装”按钮。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-249">Select the **Install** button.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-250">成功安装后，你将在 Microsoft Edge Beta 的"所有应用"列表中找到"“开始”菜单"作为单独的条目。 </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-250">After successful install, you'll find Microsoft Edge Beta, Dev, or Canary as a separate entry in the **All apps** list of the Start menu.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-251">**通过具有 Windows 设备门户 ([的电脑进行](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/develop/platform-capabilities-and-apis/using-the-windows-device-portal#setting-up-hololens-to-use-windows-device-portal) 安装需要在应用程序上启用开发人员HoloLens 2)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-251">**Install via PC with Windows Device Portal (requires [developer mode](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/develop/platform-capabilities-and-apis/using-the-windows-device-portal#setting-up-hololens-to-use-windows-device-portal) to be enabled on HoloLens 2)**</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-252">在电脑上，访问 [Edge 预览体验成员下载页](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com/download)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-252">On your PC, visit the [Edge Insider download page](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com/download).</span></span>

  1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-257">成功安装后，你将在 Microsoft Edge Beta 的"所有应用"列表中找到"“开始”菜单"作为单独的条目。 </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-257">After successful install, you'll find Microsoft Edge Beta, Dev, or Canary as a separate entry in the **All apps** list of the Start menu.</span></span>

#### <a name="using-wdac-to-block-new-microsoft-edge"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-258">使用 WDAC 阻止新Microsoft Edge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-258">Using WDAC to block new Microsoft Edge</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-259">对于希望更新 [WDAC](windows-defender-application-control-wdac.md) 策略以阻止新的 Microsoft Edge 应用的 IT 管理员，需要将以下内容添加到策略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-259">For IT Admins looking to update their [WDAC policy](windows-defender-application-control-wdac.md) to block the new Microsoft Edge app, you'll need to add the following to your policy.</span></span>

``` <Deny ID="ID_DENY_D_3_0" FriendlyName="C:\Data\Programs FileRule" PackageVersion="65535.65535.65535.65535" FileName="msedge.exe" /> ```

#### <a name="managing-endpoints-for-the-new-microsoft-edge"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-260">管理新终结点的Microsoft Edge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-260">Managing endpoints for the new Microsoft Edge</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-261">某些环境可能需要考虑网络限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-261">Some environments may have network restrictions to account for as a consideration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-262">若要确保顺利使用新 Edge，请 [启用这些 Microsoft 终结点。](https://docs.microsoft.com/deployedge/microsoft-edge-security-endpoints)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-262">To ensure a smooth experience with the new Edge please [enable these Microsoft endpoints.](https://docs.microsoft.com/deployedge/microsoft-edge-security-endpoints)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-263">详细了解 [HoloLens 当前可用的终结点](hololens-offline.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-263">Read more about the currently available [endpoints for HoloLens](hololens-offline.md).</span></span>

### <a name="install-web-apps"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-264">安装 Web 应用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-264">Install web apps</span></span>
 > [!Note]
><span data-ttu-id="c256e-265">从 [Windows Holographic 版本 21H1](hololens-release-notes.md#windows-holographic-version-21h1)起，将不再预安装 Office Web 应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-265">As of [Windows Holographic, version 21H1](hololens-release-notes.md#windows-holographic-version-21h1), the Office web app will no longer be pre-installed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-266">可以使用新的 Edge 将 Web 应用与 Microsoft Store一起安装。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-266">You can use the new Edge to install web apps alongside Microsoft Store apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-267">例如，可以安装 Microsoft Office Web 应用来查看和编辑 SharePoint 或 OneDrive 上托管的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-267">For example, you can install the Microsoft Office web app to view and edit files hosted on SharePoint or OneDrive.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-268">若要安装 Office Web 应用，请访问并选择地址栏中的"应用可用"或"安装 https://www.office.com **Office"** 按钮。 </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-268">To install the Office web app, visit https://www.office.com and select the **App Available** or **Install Office** button in the address bar.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-269">选择 **"安装** "以确认。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-269">Select **Install** to confirm.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-270">仅当 HoloLens 2 具有活动 internet 连接时，Office web 应用功能才可用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-270">Office web app functionality is only available when your HoloLens 2 has an active internet connection.</span></span>

### <a name="webxr-and-360-viewer"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-271">WebXR 和360查看器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-271">WebXR and 360 Viewer</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-272">新的 Microsoft Edge 包含对 WebXR 的支持，这是 (替换 WebVR) 的新标准，用于创建沉浸式 web 体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-272">The new Microsoft Edge includes support for WebXR, which is the new standard for creating immersive web experiences (replacing WebVR).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-273">许多沉浸式 web 体验在设计上都是使用 VR (它们将视图的字段替换为虚拟环境) ，但 HoloLens 2 也支持这些体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-273">Many immersive web experiences were designed with VR in mind (they replace your field of view with a virtual environment), but these experiences are also supported by HoloLens 2.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-274">WebXR 标准还启用了使用物理环境的扩充和混合现实沉浸式 web 体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-274">The WebXR standard also enables augmented and mixed reality immersive web experiences that use your physical environment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-275">随着开发人员花更多时间来 WebXR，我们预计新增加和混合现实的丰富体验将会为 HoloLens 2 客户尝试！</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-275">As developers spend more time with WebXR, we anticipate new augmented and mixed reality immersive experiences will arrive for HoloLens 2 customers to try!</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-276">360查看器扩展基于 WebXR，并在新的 Microsoft Edge 和 HoloLens 2 上自动安装。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-276">The 360 Viewer extension is built on WebXR and automatically installs alongside the new Microsoft Edge on HoloLens 2.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-277">此 web 扩展使你能够在360度视频中从而深入了解。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-277">This web extension gives you the ability to immerse yourself in 360-degree videos.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-278">YouTube 提供最大程度的360视频，因此我们鼓励你从这里开始。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-278">YouTube offers the largest selection of 360 videos, so we encourage you to start there.</span></span>

#### <a name="how-to-use-webxr"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-279">如何使用 WebXR</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-279">How to use WebXR</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-280">导航到支持 WebXR 的网站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-280">Navigate to a website with WebXR support.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-281">选择网站上的 " **输入** "。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-281">Select the **Enter VR** button on the website.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-282">此按钮的位置和视觉表示形式可能因网站而异，但它看起来可能类似于：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-282">The location and visual representation of this button may vary per website, but it may look similar to:</span></span>

    ![输入 VR 按钮示例](images/75px-enter-vr.png)

1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-284">首次尝试在特定域上启动 WebXR 体验时，浏览器将要求同意输入沉浸式视图，并选择 " **允许**"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-284">The first time you try to launch a WebXR experience on a specific domain, the browser will ask for consent to enter an immersive view, select **Allow**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-285">使用 [HoloLens 2 手势](hololens2-basic-usage.md#the-hand-tracking-frame) 来处理体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-285">Use [HoloLens 2 gestures](hololens2-basic-usage.md#the-hand-tracking-frame) to manipulate the experience.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-286">如果体验没有 **退出** 按钮，请使用 [开始手势](hololens2-basic-usage.md#start-gesture) 返回 home。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-286">If the experience doesn't have an **Exit** button, use the [Start gesture](hololens2-basic-usage.md#start-gesture) to return home.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-287">**建议的 WebXR 示例**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-287">**Recommended WebXR samples**</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-288">360查看器 (参阅下一节) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-288">360 Viewer (see next section)</span></span>
- [<span data-ttu-id="c256e-289">XR 恐龙</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-289">XR Dinosaurs</span></span>](https://www.xrdinosaurs.com/)
- [<span data-ttu-id="c256e-290">Barista Express</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-290">Barista Express</span></span>](https://constructarca.de/game/barista-express/)
- [<span data-ttu-id="c256e-291">WebXR 绘制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-291">WebXR Paint</span></span>](https://threejs.org/examples/webxr_vr_paint.html)

#### <a name="how-to-use-360-viewer"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-292">如何使用 360 查看器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-292">How to use 360 Viewer</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-293">导航到 YouTube 上的 360 度视频。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-293">Navigate to a 360-degree video on YouTube.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-294">在视频帧中，选择混合现实头戴显示设备按钮：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-294">In the video frame, select the mixed reality headset button:</span></span>

    ![用于激活 360 查看器的按钮](images/enter-360-viewer.jpg)

1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-296">首次尝试在特定的域上启动 360 查看器时，浏览器会请求同意进入沉浸式视图。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-296">The first time you try to launch 360 Viewer on a specific domain, the browser will ask for consent to enter an immersive view.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-297">选择“允许”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-297">Select **Allow**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-298">[通过敲](hololens2-basic-usage.md#select-using-air-tap) 击打开播放控件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-298">[Air tap](hololens2-basic-usage.md#select-using-air-tap) to bring up the playback controls.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-299">使用 [手部光线和敲](hololens2-basic-usage.md#select-using-air-tap) 击播放/暂停、跳过向前/后退、打开/关闭字幕或停止体验 (退出沉浸式) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-299">Use [hand rays and air tap](hololens2-basic-usage.md#select-using-air-tap) to play/pause, skip forward/back, turn captions on/off, or stop the experience (which exits the immersive view).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-300">处于非活动状态几秒钟后，播放控件将消失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-300">The playback controls will disappear after a few seconds of inactivity.</span></span>

#### <a name="top-webxr-and-360-viewer-known-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-301">WebXR 和 360 查看器已知问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-301">Top WebXR and 360 Viewer known issues</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-302">根据 WebXR 体验的复杂性，帧速率可能会下降或降低。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-302">Depending on the complexity of the WebXR experience, the framerate may drop or stutter.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-303">默认情况下，不支持 WebXR 中的铰接式手部。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-303">Support for articulated hand joints in WebXR is not enabled by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-304">开发人员可以通过打开"WebXR 手部输入" `edge://flags` 来启用支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-304">Developers can enable support via `edge://flags` by turning on "WebXR Hand Input."</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-305">YouTube 外网站的 360 个视频可能无法如预期工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-305">360 videos from websites other than YouTube may not work as expected.</span></span>

#### <a name="providing-feedback-on-webxr-and-360-viewer"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-306">提供有关 WebXR 和 360 查看器的反馈</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-306">Providing feedback on WebXR and 360 Viewer</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-307">请通过新文章中的"发送反馈"功能与我们的团队共享Microsoft Edge。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-307">Please share feedback and bugs with our team via the **Send Feedback** feature in the new Microsoft Edge.</span></span>

### <a name="new-settings-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-308">新建设置应用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-308">New Settings app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-309">在此版本中，我们将引入新版本的"设置"应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-309">With this release, we're introducing a new version of the Settings app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-310">新的"设置"应用包括以下HoloLens 2新功能和扩展设置：声音、电源 & 睡眠、网络 & Internet、应用、帐户、轻松访问等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-310">The new Settings app includes new features and expanded settings for HoloLens 2 in the following areas: Sound, Power & sleep, Network & Internet, Apps, Accounts, Ease of Access, and more.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-311">由于新的 "设置" 应用不同于旧的 "设置" 应用，因此在更新时将删除以前在环境中放置的任何设置窗口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-311">Because the new Settings app is distinct from the legacy Settings app, any Settings windows you previously placed around your environment will be removed upon update.</span></span>

![新设置应用主页](images/new-settings-app.png)

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-313">**新功能和设置**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-313">**New features and settings**</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-314">设置搜索：使用关键字或设置的名称从 "设置" 主页搜索设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-314">Settings search: search for settings from the Settings homepage using keywords or the setting's name.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-315">系统 > 声音：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-315">System > Sound:</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="c256e-316">输入和输出音频设备：例如，单独选择输入和输出音频设备 (例如，通过蓝牙耳机收听音频，或使用 USB C 麦克风进行音频输入) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-316">Input and output audio devices: independently choose your input and output audio devices (for example, listen to audio via Bluetooth headphones or use a USB-C microphone for audio input).</span></span>
    > [!NOTE]
    > <span data-ttu-id="c256e-317">HoloLens 2 不支持蓝牙麦克风。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-317">Bluetooth microphones are not supported by HoloLens 2.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="c256e-318">应用卷：独立调整每个应用的音量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-318">App volume: independently adjust the volume of each app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-319">请参阅 [每个应用音量控制](#per-app-volume-control)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-319">See [per app volume control](#per-app-volume-control).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-320">系统 > Power & 睡眠：在设备处于非活动状态一段时间后，选择设备应进入睡眠状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-320">System > Power & sleep: choose when the device should go to sleep after a period of inactivity.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-321">系统 > 电池：手动启用节电模式，或设置节电模式自动开启的电池阈值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-321">System > Battery: manually enable battery saver mode or set a battery threshold at which point battery saver mode turns on automatically.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-322">设备 > USB：默认情况下，可以禁用 USB 连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-322">Devices > USB: you can disable USB connections by default.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-323">网络 & Internet：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-323">Network & Internet:</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="c256e-324">USB 以太网适配器现在会显示在网络 & Internet 中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-324">USB-C Ethernet adapters will now appear in Network & Internet.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="c256e-325">现在可以使用 USB-C 以太网适配器设置，包括其 IP 地址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-325">USB-C Ethernet adapter settings are now available, including its IP address.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="c256e-326">你现在可以在 HoloLens 2 上启用飞行模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-326">You can now enable airplane mode on HoloLens 2.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-327">应用：可以重置用于文件和链接类型的默认应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-327">Apps: you can reset the default apps used for file and link types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-328">有关详细信息，请参阅 [默认应用选取器](#default-app-picker)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-328">For more information see [Default app picker](#default-app-picker).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-329">帐户 > 其他用户：设备所有者可以添加用户、将标准用户升级到设备所有者、将设备所有者降级为标准用户以及删除用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-329">Accounts > Other users: device owners can add users, upgrade standard users to device owners, downgrade device owners to standard users, and remove users.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-330">易于访问：更改文本大小和一些视觉效果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-330">Ease of Access: change text size and some visual effects.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-331">**已知问题**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-331">**Known issues**</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-332">以前放置的"设置"窗口将被删除 (请参阅上面的) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-332">Previously placed Settings windows will be removed (see note above).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-333">无法再使用"设置"应用重命名设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-333">You can no longer rename your device with the Settings app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-334">IT 管理员可以通过使用设备名称模板Windows Autopilot MDM [DevDetail CSP](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/devdetail-csp) Ext/Microsoft/DNSComputerName [HoloLens 2](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens2-autopilot)重命名设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-334">IT admins can rename devices by using the [Windows Autopilot for HoloLens 2](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens2-autopilot) device name template or the MDM [DevDetail CSP](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/devdetail-csp) Ext/Microsoft/DNSComputerName node.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-335">"以太网"页显示一个 ("UsbNcm") 虚拟以太网设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-335">The Ethernet page shows a virtual Ethernet device ("UsbNcm") at all times.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-336">由于 UWP 适配器层Microsoft Edge Win32 桌面应用程序的性质，新应用程序的电池使用情况可能不准确， (预计不会) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-336">Battery usage for the new Microsoft Edge may not be accurate, due to its nature as a Win32 desktop application supported by a UWP adapter layer (no fix anticipated soon).</span></span>

#### <a name="display-color-calibration"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-337">显示颜色校准</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-337">Display color calibration</span></span>



<span data-ttu-id="c256e-338">借助此新设置，可以选择其他颜色配置文件来显示HoloLens 2配置文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-338">With this new setting, you can select an alternative color profile for your HoloLens 2 display.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-339">这有助于颜色看起来更准确，尤其是在较低的显示亮度级别。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-339">This may help colors appear more accurate, especially at lower display brightness levels.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-340">可以在"设置"应用的"系统校准"页上找到显示颜色>校准。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-340">Display color calibration can be found in the Settings app, on the System > Calibration page.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-341">由于此设置将新的颜色配置文件保存到显示固件，因此它是每个设备设置 (，并非每个用户帐户) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-341">Because this setting saves a new color profile to your display firmware, it is a per-device setting (and not unique to each user account).</span></span>

##### <a name="how-to-use-display-color-calibration"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-342">如何使用显示颜色校准</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-342">How to use display color calibration</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-343">启动"**设置"** 应用并导航到 **"系统>校准"。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-343">Launch the **Settings** app and navigate to **System > Calibration**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-344">在 **"显示颜色校准"** 下，选择 **"运行显示颜色校准"** 按钮。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-344">Under **Display color calibration**, select the **Run display color calibration** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-345">显示颜色校准体验将启动，鼓励你确保视器处于正确的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-345">The display color calibration experience will launch and encourage you to make sure your visor is in the correct position.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-346">在继续浏览指令对话框后，显示将自动灰显为 30% 的亮度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-346">After you proceed through the instruction dialog boxes, your display will automatically be dimmed to 30% brightness.</span></span>
    > [!TIP]
    > <span data-ttu-id="c256e-347">如果在环境中看到灰色场景时遇到问题，可以使用设备左侧的亮度按钮手动HoloLens 2亮度级别。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-347">If you're having trouble seeing the dimmed scene in your environment, you can manually adjust the brightness level of HoloLens 2 using the brightness buttons on the left side of the device.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-348">选择按钮 1-6 可立即试用每个颜色配置文件，并找到最适合你眼睛的颜色配置文件 (这通常意味着有助于场景显示最中性、灰度模式和外观色调按预期呈现的配置文件。) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-348">Select buttons 1-6 to instantly try out each color profile, and find one that looks the best to your eyes (this usually means the profile that helps the scene appear most neutral, with the grayscale pattern and skin tones looking as expected.)</span></span>

    ![显示颜色校准场景](images/color-cal-ui.png)
    
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-350">当你对所选配置文件满意时，选择 " **保存 & 退出** " 按钮</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-350">When you're happy with the selected profile, select the **Save & Exit** button</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-351">如果你不想进行更改，请选择 " **取消 & 退出** " 按钮，你的更改将恢复</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-351">If you prefer not to make changes, select the **Cancel & Exit** button and your changes will be reverted</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-352">下面是使用显示颜色校准设置时需要注意的一些有用提示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-352">Here are some helpful tips to keep in mind while using the display color calibration setting:</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="c256e-353">你可以根据需要从设置重新运行显示颜色校准</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-353">You can re-run display color calibration from Settings whenever you'd like</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="c256e-354">如果设备上的任何人以前使用了更改颜色配置文件的设置，则最近更改的日期/时间将反映在 "设置" 页上</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-354">If anyone on the device has previously used the setting to change color profiles, the date/time of the most recent change will be reflected on the Settings page</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="c256e-355">重新运行 "显示颜色校准" 时，将突出显示以前保存的颜色配置文件，并且不会显示配置文件 0 (因为配置文件0表示显示的原始颜色配置文件) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-355">When you re-run display color calibration, the color profile that was previously saved will be highlighted and Profile 0 will not appear (as Profile 0 represents the display's original color profile)</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="c256e-356">如果要恢复到显示的原始颜色配置文件，可从 "设置" 页上 (参阅 [如何重置颜色配置文件](#how-to-reset-color-profile)) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-356">If you want to revert to the display's original color profile, you can do so from the Settings page (see [how to reset color profile](#how-to-reset-color-profile))</span></span>

##### <a name="how-to-reset-color-profile"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-357">如何重置颜色配置文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-357">How to reset color profile</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-358">如果不满意保存到 HoloLens 2 的自定义颜色配置文件，则可以还原设备的原始颜色配置文件：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-358">If you're unhappy with the custom color profile saved to your HoloLens 2, you can restore the device's original color profile:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-359">启动 " **设置** " 应用，并导航到 " **系统 > 校准**"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-359">Launch the **Settings** app and navigate to **System > Calibration**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-360">在 " **显示颜色校准**" 下，选择 " **重置为默认颜色配置文件** " 按钮。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-360">Under **Display color calibration**, select the **Reset to default color profile** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-361">当对话框打开时，如果已准备好重新启动 HoloLens 2 并应用所做的更改，请选择 " **重新启动** "。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-361">When the dialog box opens, select **Restart** if you're ready to restart HoloLens 2 and apply your changes.</span></span>

#### <a name="top-display-color-calibration-known-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-362">顶部显示颜色校准已知问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-362">Top display color calibration known issues</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-363">在 "设置" 页上，在重新加载设置页面之前，提示你上次更改颜色配置文件的状态字符串将过期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-363">On the Settings page, the status string that tells you when the color profile was last changed will be out of date until you reload that page of Settings.</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="c256e-364">解决方法：选择其他设置页，然后重新选择校准页。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-364">Workaround: Select another Settings page and then re-select the Calibration page.</span></span>

#### <a name="default-app-picker"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-365">默认应用选取器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-365">Default app picker</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-366">当你激活超链接或打开具有多个已安装的应用程序的文件类型（该应用程序支持该类型）时，你将看到一个新窗口打开，提示你选择哪个已安装的应用程序应处理文件或链接类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-366">When you activate a hyperlink or open a file type with more than one installed app, which supports it, you will see a new window open prompting you to select which installed app should handle the file or link type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-367">在此窗口中，你还可以选择让选定的应用处理文件或链接类型 "一次" 或 "始终"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-367">In this window, you can also choose to have the selected app handle the file or link type "Once" or "Always."</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-368">如果选择"始终"，但以后想要更改处理特定文件或链接类型的应用，可以在"设置"或"应用"> **重置保存的默认值**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-368">If you choose "Always" but later want to change which app handles a particular file or link type, you can reset your saved defaults in **Settings > Apps**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-369">滚动到页面底部，选择"文件类型的默认应用"和/或"链接类型的默认应用"下的"清除"按钮。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-369">Scroll to the bottom of the page and select the **Clear** button under "Default apps for file types" and/or "Default apps for link types."</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-370">与台式电脑上的类似设置不同，无法重置单个文件类型默认值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-370">Unlike the similar setting on desktop PCs, you can't reset individual file type defaults.</span></span>

#### <a name="per-app-volume-control"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-371">每个应用音量控制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-371">Per app volume control</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-372">现在在此 Windows 内部版本中，用户可以手动调整每个应用的卷级别。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-372">Now in this Windows build, users can manually adjust the volume level of each app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-373">这样，用户可以更好地专注于所需的应用，或在使用多个应用时更好地听到这些应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-373">This allows for users to better focus on the apps that they need to, or better hear when using multiple apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-374">例如，需要关闭一个应用的数量，同时调用另一个人在另一个应用中进行远程协助。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-374">Such as needing to turn down volume of one app while calling another person for remote assistance in another.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-375">若要设置单个应用的音量，请导航 **到"设置** 系统声音"，并在"高级声音选项"下  ->    ->  选择"**应用音量和设备首选项"。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-375">To set the volume of an individual app navigate to **Settings** -> **System** -> **Sound**, and under Advanced sound options select **App volume and device preferences**.</span></span>

 <img alt="App volume and device preferences." src="./images/volume-per-app.jpg" width="500" height="250" />

#### <a name="swipe-to-type"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-376">轻扫以键入</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-376">Swipe to type</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-377">一些客户发现，通过轻扫要键入的单词的形状，在虚拟键盘上"键入"速度更快，我们正在预览全息键盘的此功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-377">Some customers find it faster to "type" on virtual keyboards by swiping the shape of the word they intend to type, and we're previewing this feature for the holographic keyboard.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-378">可以通过将手指的尖通过全息键盘的平面，轻扫该单词的形状，然后从键盘平面中收回手指的提示，一次轻扫一个词。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-378">You can swipe one word at a time by passing the tip of your finger through the plane of the holographic keyboard, swiping the shape of the word, and then withdrawing the tip of your finger from the plane of the keyboard.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-379">通过从键盘上删除单词之间的手指，无需按空格键即可轻扫后续字词。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-379">You can swipe follow up words without needing to press the space bar by removing your finger from the keyboard between words.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-380">如果在键盘上手指移动后看到轻扫线索，则你会知道该功能正在工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-380">You will know the feature is working if you see a swipe trail following your finger's movement on the keyboard.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-381">请注意，此功能可能难以使用和掌握，因为全息键盘的性质与手机显示设备不同， (对手指的抵御) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-381">Please note, this feature can be tricky to use and master because of the nature of a holographic keyboard where you don't feel resistance against your finger (unlike a mobile phone display).</span></span> 

### <a name="power-menu-from-start"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-382">"开始"中的电源菜单</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-382">Power menu from Start</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-383">允许用户注销、关闭和重启设备的新菜单。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-383">A new menu that allows the user to sign out, shut down and restart the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-384">HoloLens “开始”屏幕指示系统更新何时可用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-384">An indicator in the HoloLens Start screen that shows when a system update is available.</span></span>

#### <a name="how-to-use"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-385">如何使用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-385">How to use</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-386">使用 [开始手势](hololens2-basic-usage.md#start-gesture) 或说 "前往开始时间" 打开 HoloLens 开始屏幕。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-386">Open the HoloLens Start screen using the [Start gesture](hololens2-basic-usage.md#start-gesture) or saying "Go to Start".</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-387">请注意，用户配置文件图片旁边的省略号图标 ( ) ：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-387">Notice the ellipsis icon (...) next to the user profile picture:</span></span>

   <img alt="ser context dots, ..." src="./images/powertransition_icon_default_cropped.png" width="586" height="330" />

3. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-388">使用手或语音命令 "电源" 选择用户配置文件图片。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-388">Select the user profile picture using your hands or the voice command "Power".</span></span>

4. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-389">此时将显示一个菜单，其中包含用于注销、重新启动或关闭设备的选项：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-389">A menu appears with options to Sign out, Restart or Shut down the device:</span></span>

5. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-390">选择要注销、重启或关闭 HoloLens 的菜单选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-390">Select the menu options to sign out, restart or shut down your HoloLens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-391">"注销" 选项可能不可用，如果设备设置为 [单一 Microsoft 帐户 (MSA) 或本地帐户](hololens-identity.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-391">The Sign out option might not be available, if the device is set up for a [single Microsoft Account (MSA) or local account](hololens-identity.md).</span></span>

6. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-392">通过触摸任何其他位置或使用开始手势关闭开始菜单，消除菜单。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-392">Dismiss the menu by touching anywhere else or closing the Start menu with the Start gesture.</span></span>

#### <a name="update-indicator"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-393">更新指示器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-393">Update indicator</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-394">当更新可用时，省略号图标会亮起，指示重新启动将会安装更新。菜单选项还会更改，以反映更新的状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-394">When an update is available, the ellipsis icon will light up to indicate that a restart will install the update The menu options also change to reflect the presence of the update.</span></span><br/><br/>

### <a name="multiple-users-listed-on-sign-in-screen"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-395">登录屏幕上列出了多个用户</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-395">Multiple users listed on Sign in screen</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-396">以前的登录屏幕只显示最近登录的用户，以及 "其他用户" 入口点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-396">Previously the Sign In screen showed only the most recently signed in user, as well as an 'Other user' entry point.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-397">如果有多个用户登录到设备，我们已收到客户反馈。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-397">We have received customer feedback that this not sufficient if multiple users have signed into the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-398">它们仍需要重新键入其用户名等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-398">They were still required to retype their username etc.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-399">在此 Windows 版本中引入的，选择位于 "PIN 输入" 字段右侧的 " **其他用户** " 时，"登录" 屏幕将显示多个以前登录到设备的用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-399">Introduced in this Windows build, when selecting **Other user** which is located to the right of the PIN entry field, the Sign in screen will display multiple users with have previously signed into the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-400">这允许用户选择其用户配置文件，然后使用他们的 Windows Hello 凭据进行登录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-400">This allows users to select their user profile and then sign-in using their Windows Hello credentials.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-401">还可以通过 " **添加帐户** " 按钮将新用户添加到该设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-401">A new user can also be added to the device from this Other users page via the **Add account** button.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-402">在 "其他用户" 菜单中，"其他用户" 按钮将显示最后一个登录到设备的用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-402">When in the Other users menu, the Other users button will display the last user signed into the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-403">选择此按钮可返回到此用户的登录屏幕。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-403">Select this button to return to the Sign in screen for this user.</span></span>

### <a name="usb-c-external-microphone-support"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-406">USB-C 外部麦克风支持</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-406">USB-C External Microphone Support</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-407">插入 **USB 麦克风不会自动将其设置为输入设备**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-407">Plugging in **a USB mic will not automatically set it as the input device**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-408">在插入一组 USB-C 耳机时，用户将观察到耳机的音频将自动重定向到耳机，但 HoloLens OS 将内部麦克风阵列的优先级设置为高于任何其他输入设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-408">When plugging in a set of USB-C headphones users will observe that the headphone's audio will automatically be redirected to the headphones, but the HoloLens OS prioritizes the internal microphone array above any other input device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-409">**若要使用 USB-C 麦克风，请执行以下步骤。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-409">**In order to use a USB-C microphone follow the steps below.**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-410">用户可以使用"声音设置"面板选择已连接 USB-C **的外部** 麦克风。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-410">Users can select USB-C connected external microphones using the **Sound** settings panel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-411">USB-C 麦克风可用于通话、录制等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-411">USB-C microphones can be used for calling, recording, etc.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-412">打开"**设置"** 应用，然后选择"**系统**  >  **声音"。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-412">Open the **Settings** app and select **System** > **Sound**.</span></span>

![声音设置](images/usbc-mic-1.jpg)

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-414">若要将外部麦克风与 **Remote Assist，用户** 需要单击"管理声音设备"超链接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-414">To use external microphones with **Remote Assist**, users will need to click the “Manage sound devices” hyperlink.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-415">然后，使用下拉列表将外部麦克风设置为"默认" **或** " **通信默认值"。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-415">Then use the drop-down to set the external microphone as either **Default** or **Communications Default.**</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-416">选择 **"** 默认"意味着外部麦克风将在所有位置使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-416">Choosing **Default** means that the external microphone will be used everywhere.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-417">选择 **"** 通信默认值"意味着外部麦克风将用于 Remote Assist和其他通信应用，但 HoloLens 麦克风阵列仍可用于其他任务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-417">Choosing **Communications Default** means that the external microphone will be used in Remote Assist and other communications apps, but the HoloLens mic array may still be used for other tasks.</span></span>

#### <a name="what-about-bluetooth-microphone-support"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-420">蓝牙麦克风支持呢？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-420">What about Bluetooth microphone support?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-421">遗憾的是，蓝牙麦克风目前仍不受 HoloLens 2。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-421">Unfortunately Bluetooth microphones are still not currently supported on HoloLens 2.</span></span>

#### <a name="troubleshooting-usb-c-microphones"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-422">USB-C 麦克风疑难解答</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-422">Troubleshooting USB-C microphones</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-423">请注意，某些 USB-C 麦克风错误地将自身报告为 *麦克风和扬声器* 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-423">Be aware that some USB-C microphones incorrectly report themselves as both a microphone *and* a speaker.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-424">这是麦克风的问题，而不是 HoloLens 的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-424">This is a problem with the microphone and not with HoloLens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-425">将其中一个麦克风插入 HoloLens 时，可能会丢失声音。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-425">When plugging one of these microphones into HoloLens, sound may be lost.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-426">幸运的是，有一个简单的修补程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-426">Fortunately there is a simple fix.</span></span>  

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-427">在 "**设置**  ->  **系统**  ->  **声音**" 中，显式设置内置扬声器 **(模拟功能音频驱动程序)** 作为 **默认设备**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-427">In **Settings** -> **System** -> **Sound**, explicitly set the built-in speakers **(Analog Feature Audio Driver)** as the **Default device**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-428">即使删除了麦克风并稍后重新连接，HoloLens 也应记住此设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-428">HoloLens should remember this setting even if the microphone is removed and reconnected later.</span></span>

![USB-C 麦克风疑难解答](images/usbc-mic-4.png)

### <a name="visitor-auto-logon-for-kiosks"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-430">网亭的访问者自动登录</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-430">Visitor Auto logon for Kiosks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-431">这项新功能使访问者帐户上的自动登录可用于展台模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-431">This new feature enables the auto logon on Visitor accounts to be used for Kiosk modes.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-432">对于非 AAD 配置，为访问者自动登录配置设备：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-432">For a non-AAD configuration, to configure a device for visitor auto-logon:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-433">创建一个预配包，其中：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-433">Create a provisioning package that:</span></span>
    1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-434">将 **运行时设置 AssignedAccess** 配置为允许访问者帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-434">Configures **Runtime settings/AssignedAccess** to allow Visitor accounts.</span></span>
    1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-435">（可选）在 MDM **(运行时设置/工作区/注册)** 中注册设备，以便以后可以对其进行管理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-435">Optionally enrolls the device in MDM **(Runtime settings/Workplace/Enrollments)** so that it can be managed later.</span></span>
    1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-436">不创建本地帐户</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-436">Do not create a local account</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-437">[应用设置包](hololens-provisioning.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-437">[Apply the provisioning package](hololens-provisioning.md).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-438">对于 AAD 配置，用户可以立即获得类似于此的内容，而无需进行此更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-438">For an AAD configuration, users can achieve something similar to this today without this change.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-439">为展台模式配置的 AAD 加入设备可以通过在登录屏幕上点击一次按钮，登录访问者帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-439">AAD joined devices configured for kiosk mode can sign in a Visitor account with a single button tap from the sign in screen.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-440">登录到访问者帐户后，在从 "开始" 菜单中显式注销访问者或重新启动设备之前，该设备将不会提示登录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-440">Once signed in to the visitor account, the device will not prompt for sign in again until the Visitor is explicitly signed out from the start menu or the device is restarted.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-441">可以通过 [自定义 OMA URI](https://docs.microsoft.com/mem/intune/configuration/custom-settings-windows-10) 策略来管理访问者自动登录：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-441">Visitor Auto logon can be managed via [custom OMA-URI](https://docs.microsoft.com/mem/intune/configuration/custom-settings-windows-10) policy:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-442">URI 值：./Device/Vendor/MSFT/MixedReality/VisitorAutoLogon</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-442">URI value: ./Device/Vendor/MSFT/MixedReality/VisitorAutoLogon</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="c256e-443">策略</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-443">Policy</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="c256e-444">描述</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-444">Description</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="c256e-445">配置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-445">Configurations</span></span>  |
|---|---|---|
| <span data-ttu-id="c256e-446">MixedReality/VisitorAutoLogon</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-446">MixedReality/VisitorAutoLogon</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="c256e-447">允许访问者自动登录到展台</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-447">Allows for a Visitor to Auto logon to a Kiosk</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="c256e-448">1 (是) ，0 (否，默认值为 ) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-448">1 (Yes), 0 (No, default.)</span></span>  |

### <a name="use-the-new-settings-and-edge-apps-in-kiosk-modes"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-449">在展台模式下使用新的设置和 Edge 应用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-449">Use the new Settings and Edge apps in Kiosk modes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-450">在展台 [中](hololens-kiosk.md)包括应用时，IT 管理员通常会将应用添加到展台，但使用应用用户模型 ID (AUMID) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-450">When including apps in [Kiosks](hololens-kiosk.md), an IT Admin often adds the app to the Kiosk but using it's App User Model ID (AUMID).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-451">由于设置应用和 Microsoft Edge 应用都被视为新应用，并且不同于使用这些应用的 AUMID 的较旧应用展台，因此需要更新以使用新的 AUMID。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-451">Because both the Settings app and Microsoft Edge app are considered new apps and different than the older apps Kiosks that use AUMIDs for those apps will need to be updated to use the new AUMID.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-452">修改展台以包含新应用时，建议在新的 AUMID 中添加 ，并保留旧应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-452">When modifying a Kiosk to include the new apps, we recommend adding in the new AUMID as well as leaving the old one.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-453">当用户更新 OS 且无需接收新策略以继续使用展台时，这将创建一个简单的转换。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-453">This will create an easy transition when users update the OS and won't need to receive new policies to keep using the Kiosk as intended.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="c256e-454">应用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-454">App</span></span>                    | <span data-ttu-id="c256e-455">AUMID</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-455">AUMID</span></span>                                                  |
|------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="c256e-456">旧设置应用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-456">Old Settings App</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="c256e-457">HolographicSystemSettings_cw5n1h2txyewy！应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-457">HolographicSystemSettings_cw5n1h2txyewy!App</span></span>            |
| <span data-ttu-id="c256e-458">新建设置应用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-458">New Settings App</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="c256e-459">BAEAEF15-9BAB-47FC-800B-ACECAD2AE94B_cw5n1h2txyewy！应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-459">BAEAEF15-9BAB-47FC-800B-ACECAD2AE94B_cw5n1h2txyewy!App</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="c256e-460">旧 Microsoft Edge 应用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-460">Old Microsoft Edge app</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="c256e-461">Microsoft.MicrosoftEdge_8wekyb3d8bbwe!MicrosoftEdge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-461">Microsoft.MicrosoftEdge_8wekyb3d8bbwe!MicrosoftEdge</span></span>    |
| <span data-ttu-id="c256e-462">新建Microsoft Edge应用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-462">New Microsoft Edge app</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="c256e-463">Microsoft.MicrosoftEdge.Stable_8wekyb3d8bbwe！MSEDGE</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-463">Microsoft.MicrosoftEdge.Stable_8wekyb3d8bbwe!MSEDGE</span></span>    |

### <a name="kiosk-mode-behavior-changes-for-handling-of-failures"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-464">展台模式行为更改，用于处理故障</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-464">Kiosk mode behavior changes for handling of failures</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-465">在较早的生成中，如果设备具有展台配置（这是全局分配的访问权限和 AAD 团队成员分配的访问权限的组合）时，如果确定 AAD 组成员身份失败，用户将看到"开始"[](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens-kiosk#kiosk-mode-behavior-changes-for-handling-of-failures)菜单中未显示任何内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-465">In older builds, if a device had a kiosk configuration, which is a combination of both global assigned access and AAD group member assigned access, if determining AAD group membership failed, the user would see “[nothing shown in start](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens-kiosk#kiosk-mode-behavior-changes-for-handling-of-failures)” menu.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-466">从此 Windows 版本开始，展台体验将回退到全局展台配置 (在 AAD 组展台模式) 发生故障时出现。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-466">Starting in this Windows release, the kiosk experience will fallback to global kiosk configuration (if present) in case of failures during AAD group kiosk mode.</span></span>

### <a name="new-settings-uris-for-page-settings-visibility"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-467">页面设置可见性的新设置 URI</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-467">New Settings URIs for Page Settings Visibility</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-468">在 [Windows Holographic 版本 20H2](hololens-release-notes.md#windows-holographic-version-20h2) 中，我们添加了 ["设置/PageVisibilityList"](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/policy-csp-settings#settings-pagevisibilitylist) 策略，以限制在"设置"应用中看到的页面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-468">In [Windows Holographic, version 20H2](hololens-release-notes.md#windows-holographic-version-20h2) we added the [Settings/PageVisibilityList policy](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/policy-csp-settings#settings-pagevisibilitylist) to restrict the pages seen within the Settings app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-469">PageVisibilityList 是一种策略，允许 IT 管理员阻止系统设置应用中的特定页面可见或可访问，或者对除指定页面以外的所有页面执行此操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-469">PageVisibilityList is a policy that allows IT Admins to either prevent specific pages in the System Settings app from being visible or accessible, or to do so for all pages except those specified.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-470">如果访问 ["页面设置可见性"，](settings-uri-list.md)可以找到有关使用此 CSP 的说明，以及以前版本中提供的 URI 列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-470">If you visit [Page Settings Visibility](settings-uri-list.md), you can find instructions to use this CSP and the list of URIs available in previous releases.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-471">我们正在扩展可用设置 URI 的列表，IT 管理员可以管理这些 URI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-471">We are expanding upon the list of list of available Settings URIs, which IT Admins can manage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-472">其中一些 Uri 适用于新的设置应用内的新可用区域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-472">Some of these URIs are for newly available areas within the new Settings app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-473">如果你使用的是设置/PageVisibilityList 策略，请查看以下列表，并根据需要调整你允许或阻止的页面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-473">If you are using Settings/PageVisibilityList policy, review the following list and adjust your allowed or blocked pages as needed.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-474">**弃用： ms 设置：网络代理**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-474">**Deprecated: ms-settings:network-proxy**</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-475">在这些较新的版本中不推荐使用一个设置页。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-475">One settings page is deprecated in these newer builds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-476">旧的 **网络 & Internet**  >  **代理** 页面不再作为全局设置提供。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-476">The old **Network & Internet** > **Proxy** page is no longer available as a global setting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-477">新的每连接代理设置可在 **网络 & internet**  >  **wi-fi**  >  **属性** 或 **网络 & internet**  >  **以太网**  >  **属性** 下找到。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-477">The new per-connection proxy settings can be found under **Network & Internet** > **Wi-Fi** > **Properties** or **Network & Internet** > **Ethernet** > **Properties**.</span></span>

#### <a name="updated-uris"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-503">更新的 URI</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-503">Updated URIs</span></span>

- `ms-settings:windowsupdate-options`
- `ms-settings:windowsupdate-restartoptions`

### <a name="configuring-fallback-diagnostics-via-settings-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-506">通过设置应用配置回退诊断</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-506">Configuring Fallback Diagnostics via Settings app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-507">现在，在"设置应用"中，用户可以配置 [回退诊断 的行为](hololens-diagnostic-logs.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-507">Now in Settings App, a user can configure the behavior of [Fallback Diagnostics](hololens-diagnostic-logs.md).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-508">在"设置"应用中，**导航到**  ->  **"隐私疑难解答"** 页以配置此设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-508">In the Settings app navigate to **Privacy** -> **Troubleshooting** page to configure this setting.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-509">如果为设备配置了 MDM 策略，则用户将无法重写该行为。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-509">If there is MDM policy configured for the device, user will not be able to override that behavior.</span></span>  

### <a name="share-things-with-nearby-devices"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-510">与附近的设备共享内容</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-510">Share things with nearby devices</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-511">与靠近Windows 10共享内容，包括电脑和其他HoloLens 2设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-511">Share things with near by Windows 10 devices, including both PCs and other HoloLens 2 devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-512">可以在设置 **系统共享体验** 中试用它，以将文件或 URL 从  ->    ->  HoloLens 共享到电脑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-512">You can try it out in **Settings** -> **System** -> **Shared Experiences** to share files or URLs from a HoloLens to a PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-513">有关更多详细信息，请阅读有关如何在 Windows 10 中[与附近的设备共享Windows 10。](https://support.microsoft.com/windows/share-things-with-nearby-devices-in-windows-10-0efbfe40-e3e2-581b-13f4-1a0e9936c2d9)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-513">For more details read more about how to [Share things with nearby devices in Windows 10](https://support.microsoft.com/windows/share-things-with-nearby-devices-in-windows-10-0efbfe40-e3e2-581b-13f4-1a0e9936c2d9).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-514">此功能可通过 [连接/AllowConnectedDevices](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/policy-csp-connectivity#connectivity-allowconnecteddevices)进行管理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-514">This feature can be managed via [Connectivity/AllowConnectedDevices](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/policy-csp-connectivity#connectivity-allowconnecteddevices).</span></span>

### <a name="new-os-diagnostic-traces"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-515">新操作系统诊断跟踪</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-515">New OS diagnostic traces</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-516">除了在 "设置" 应用程序中使用前面的疑难解答外，还添加了新的疑难解答，同时添加了新的 OS 更新设置应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-516">In addition to the previous troubleshooters within the Settings app, a new troubleshooter has been added with the addition of the new Settings app for OS Updates.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-517">导航到 "**设置**" "  ->  **更新 &amp; 安全**  >  **疑难解答**"  >  **Windows 更新** 并选择 "**启动**"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-517">Navigate to **Settings** -> **Update &amp; Security** > **Troubleshoot** > **Windows Update** and select **Start**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-518">这样，你就可以收集跟踪，同时在操作系统更新中重现你的问题，以帮助更好地帮助你的 IT 或支持人员进行故障排除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-518">This allows you to collect traces while reproducing your issue with OS Updates to assist better in troubleshooting with your IT or support.</span></span>

### <a name="delivery-optimization-preview"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-519">传递优化预览</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-519">Delivery Optimization Preview</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-520">使用此更新，Windows 全息版可实现交付优化设置，减少从多个 HoloLens 设备下载的带宽消耗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-520">With this HoloLens update, Windows Holographic for Business enables delivery optimization settings to reduce bandwidth consumption for downloads from multiple HoloLens devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-521">此处提供了此功能以及推荐的网络配置的完整描述： [Windows 10 更新的传递优化](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/deployment/update/waas-delivery-optimization)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-521">A fuller description of this functionality along with the recommended network configuration is available here: [Delivery Optimization for Windows 10 updates](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/deployment/update/waas-delivery-optimization).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-547">✔️ [**展台的访问者自动登录：**](#visitor-auto-logon-for-kiosks)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-547">✔️ [**Visitor Auto-logon for Kiosks**](#visitor-auto-logon-for-kiosks):</span></span>

### <a name="improvements-and-fixes-in-the-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-567">更新中的改进和修复：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-567">Improvements and fixes in the update:</span></span>
