- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-570">解决了业务线应用程序安装状态报告问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-570">Fixes an issue around line of business application install status reporting.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-572">修复了可能导致在 Edge 中为日本客户键入错误符号的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-572">Fixes an issue that could lead to incorrect symbols being typed in Edge for Japanese customers.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-574">解决影响应用程序安装的更新可靠性Microsoft Edge。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-574">Addresses an update reliability impacting the installation of Microsoft Edge.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-1903---may-2021-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-579">Windows Holographic 版本 1903 - 2021 年 5 月更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-579">Windows Holographic, version 1903 - May 2021 Update</span></span>

### <a name="install-apps-on-hololens-2-via-app-installer"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-622">通过 HoloLens 2 在 应用安装程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-622">Install Apps on HoloLens 2 via App Installer</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-623">我们正在 **添加新的 (应用安装程序) ，** 以便你能够更无缝地在 HoloLens 2 设备上安装应用程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-623">We are **adding a new capability (App Installer) to allow you to install applications more seamlessly** on your HoloLens 2 devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-624">对于非 **托管设备，此功能默认为打开状态**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-624">The feature will be **on by default for unmanaged devices**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-625">为了防止企业中断，应用安装程序 **目前不适用于托管** 设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-625">To prevent disruption to enterprises, app installer will be **not be available for managed devices** at this time.</span></span>  

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-626">如果以下任一情况 **成立，则** 设备被视为"托管"设备：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-626">A device is considered “managed” if **any** of the following are true:</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-627">MDM [已注册](hololens-enroll-mdm.md)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-627">MDM [Enrolled](hololens-enroll-mdm.md)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-628">配置了 [预配包](hololens-provisioning.md)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-628">Configured with [provisioning package](hololens-provisioning.md)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-629">用户 [标识](hololens-identity.md) Azure AD</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-629">User [Identity](hololens-identity.md) is Azure AD</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-630">现在可以安装应用，而无需启用开发人员模式或设备门户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-630">You are now able to install Apps without needing to enable Developer Mode or using Device Portal.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="c256e-631">只需 (USB 或 Edge) Appx 捆绑包下载到设备，然后导航到 文件资源管理器 中的 Appx 捆绑包，以提示你启动安装。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-631">Simply download (over USB or through Edge) the Appx Bundle to your device and navigate to the Appx Bundle in the File Explorer to be prompted to kick off the installation.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="c256e-632">或者， [通过网页启动安装](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/msix/app-installer/installing-windows10-apps-web)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-632">Alternatively, [initiate an install from a web page](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/msix/app-installer/installing-windows10-apps-web).</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="c256e-633">与使用 MDM 的 LOB 应用部署功能从 Microsoft Store 或旁加载安装的应用一样，需要使用 [签名工具](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/win32/appxpkg/how-to-sign-a-package-using-signtool) 对应用进行数字签名，并且在部署应用之前，必须由 HoloLens 设备 [信任用于签署的证书](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/win32/appxpkg/how-to-sign-a-package-using-signtool#security-considerations) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-633">Just like apps you install from the Microsoft Store or sideload using MDM’s LOB App deployment capability, apps need to be digitally signed with the [Sign Tool](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/win32/appxpkg/how-to-sign-a-package-using-signtool) and the [certificate used to sign must be trusted](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/win32/appxpkg/how-to-sign-a-package-using-signtool#security-considerations) by the HoloLens device before the app can be deployed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-634">**应用程序安装说明。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-634">**Application install instructions.**</span></span>

1.  <span data-ttu-id="c256e-635">确保你的设备不被视为托管设备</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-635">Ensure that your device is not considered managed</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="c256e-636">确保你的 HoloLens 2 设备已开机并连接到你的电脑</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-636">Ensure that your HoloLens 2 device is powered on and connected to your PC</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="c256e-637">确保已登录到 HoloLens 2 设备</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-637">Ensure that you are signed into the HoloLens 2 device</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="c256e-638">在电脑上导航到自定义应用，并将 yourapp 复制到 yourdevicename\Internal Storage\Downloads。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-638">On your PC navigate to your custom app, and copy yourapp.appxbundle to yourdevicename\Internal Storage\Downloads.</span></span>   <span data-ttu-id="c256e-639">完成文件复制后，可以断开与设备的连接</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-639">After you’ve finished copying your file you can disconnect your device</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="c256e-640">在 HoloLens 2 设备上，打开 "开始" 菜单，选择 "所有应用"，然后启动 "文件资源管理器" 应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-640">From your HoloLens 2 device Open the Start Menu, select All apps and launch the File Explorer app.</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="c256e-641">导航到 "下载" 文件夹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-641">Navigate to the Downloads folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-642">你可能需要在应用程序的左侧面板上选择 "此设备"，然后导航到 "下载"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-642">You may need to on the left panel of the app select This device first, then navigate to Downloads.</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="c256e-643">选择 yourapp 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-643">Select the yourapp.appxbundle file.</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="c256e-644">应用程序安装程序将启动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-644">The App Installer will launch.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-645">选择 "安装" 按钮以安装您的应用程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-645">Select the Install button to install your app.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="c256e-646">安装完成后，安装的应用将自动启动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-646">The installed app will automatically launch upon completion of installation.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-647">可以在 [Windows 通用示例 GitHub](https://github.com/microsoft/Windows-universal-samples/tree/master/Samples) 上找到示例应用来测试此流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-647">You can find sample apps on [Windows Universal Samples GitHub](https://github.com/microsoft/Windows-universal-samples/tree/master/Samples) to test this flow.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-648">阅读有关在 [HoloLens 2 上通过应用安装程序安装应用](app-deploy-app-installer.md)的完整过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-648">Read about the full process of [installing apps on HoloLens 2 with the App Installer](app-deploy-app-installer.md).</span></span>  

![通过应用安装程序安装 MRTK 示例](images/hololens-app-installer-picture.jpg)

### <a name="improvements-and-fixes-in-the-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-650">更新中的改进和修复：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-650">Improvements and fixes in the update:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-651">手动跟踪现在可以在很多新情况下维护跟踪，这种情况先前会丢失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-651">Hand tracking now maintains tracking in many new cases where the hand previously would have been lost.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="c256e-652">在某些新情况下，只有手部位置会继续根据用户的实际手部进行更新，而其他连接则根据以前的姿势进行推断。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-652">In some of these new cases, only the palm position continues to update based on the user’s real hand, while the other joints are inferred based on a previous pose.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="c256e-653">此更改有助于提高动作（如击球、引发、跳跃和击球）的跟踪一致性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-653">This change helps improve tracking consistency in movements such as slapping, throwing, scooping, and clapping.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="c256e-654">它还有助于手靠近表面或持有对象的情况。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-654">It also helps in cases where the hand is close to a surface or holding an object.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="c256e-655">在推断手部时 [，每个联合](https://docs.microsoft.com/uwp/api/windows.perception.people.jointposeaccuracy?view=winrt-19041&preserve-view=true) 准确度值将设置为"近似"，而不是"高"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-655">When hand joints are being inferred, the [per joint accuracy](https://docs.microsoft.com/uwp/api/windows.perception.people.jointposeaccuracy?view=winrt-19041&preserve-view=true) value will be set to “Approximate” instead of “High.”</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-656">修复了帐户的 PIN 重置Azure AD显示错误"出现问题的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-656">Fixed an issue where PIN reset for Azure AD accounts would show an error "Something went wrong.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-657">启动 ET、设置应用中的 Iris、新用户或通知 toast 时，用户应看到更少的启动后 OOBE 故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-657">Users should see much less post-boot OOBE crashes when launching ET, Iris from settings app, new user, or notification toast.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-658">用户应具有来自 OOBE 的正确时区。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-658">Users should have correct time zone coming out of OOBE.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-1903--december-2020-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-659">Windows Holographic 版本 1903 - 2020 年 12 月更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-659">Windows Holographic, version 1903 – December 2020 Update</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-660">内部版本 18362.1088</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-660">Build 18362.1088</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-661">此每月质量更新不包含任何值得注意的更改，建议试用最新的 Windows Holographic 版本 20H2 – 2020 年 12 月更新和内部版本中新增的 应用安装程序 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-661">This monthly quality update doesn't contain any notable changes, we encourage you to try out our latest Windows Holographic, version 20H2 – December 2020 Update and the new App Installer feature added in the build.</span></span>


## <a name="windows-holographic-version-20h2"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-662">Windows Holographic 版本 20H2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-662">Windows Holographic, version 20H2</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-663">内部版本 19041.1128</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-663">Build 19041.1128</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-664">Windows Holographic 版本 20H2 现已发布，为用户和 IT 专业人员HoloLens 2一系列新功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-664">Windows Holographic, version 20H2 is now available and brings a great set of new features to HoloLens 2 users and IT professionals.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-665">从"自动眼定位"到"设置"中的证书管理器，到改进的展台模式功能和新的 Autopilot 设置功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-665">From Auto Eye Positioning, to Certificate Manager in Settings, to improved Kiosk Mode functionality, and new Autopilot setup capabilities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-666">此新更新使 IT 团队能够更精细地控制 HoloLens 设备的配置和管理，并为用户提供更无缝的全息体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-666">This new update enables IT teams to take more granular control to configuring and managing HoloLens devices, and offers users even more seamless holographic experiences.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-667">此最新版本是版本 2004 的每月更新，但这次我们将包含新功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-667">This latest release is a monthly update to version 2004, but this time we are including new features.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-668">主内部版本号将保持不变，Windows 更新版本 2004 (版本 19041 版本) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-668">The major build number will remain the same and Windows Update will indicate a monthly release to version 2004 (build 19041).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-669">可以在"设置"的"关于>中查看"生成号"，以确认你位于最新的可用内部版本 19041.1128+ 上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-669">You can look at your Build Number in your Settings > About screen to confirm you are on the latest available build 19041.1128+.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-670">若要更新到最新版本，请打开"设置"应用，转到"更新&安全性"，然后点击"检查更新"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-670">To update to the latest release, open the Settings app, go to Update & Security, and tap Check for Updates.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-671">有关如何管理 HoloLens 更新的详细信息，请访问 [此页](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens-updates)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-671">For more information on how to manage HoloLens updates, visit [this page](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens-updates).</span></span>

### <a name="auto-eye-position-support"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-713">自动眼部位置支持</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-713">Auto Eye Position Support</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-714">在 HoloLens 2 中，目视定位可实现准确的全息影像定位、舒适的观看体验，并改善了显示质量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-714">In HoloLens 2, eye positions enable accurate hologram positioning, comfortable viewing experience and improved display quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-715">目视位置作为眼睛跟踪计算的一部分在内部进行计算。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-715">Eye positions are computed internally as part of the eye tracking computation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-716">但是，这要求每个用户都要经历眼睛跟踪校准，即使在体验可能不需要目视输入时也是如此。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-716">However, this requires each user to go through eye tracking calibration, even when the experience might not require eye gaze input.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-717">**自动排列位置 (AEP)** 通过无交互的方式来计算用户的眼睛位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-717">**Auto Eye Position (AEP)** enables these scenarios with an interaction-free way to compute eye positions for the user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-718">自动目视位置在用户将设备置于设备上的时刻自动开始运行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-718">Auto Eye Position starts working in the background automatically from the moment the user puts the device on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-719">如果用户没有先前的目视跟踪校准，则在处理时间为 20-30 秒后，自动目视定位将开始向显示系统提供用户的眼睛位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-719">If the user does not have a prior eye tracking calibration, Auto Eye Position will start providing the user's eye positions to the display system after a processing time of 20 - 30 seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-720">用户数据不会保留在设备上，因此如果用户关闭并重新打开设备，或者设备重新启动或从睡眠状态唤醒，则此过程将重复。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-720">The user data is not persisted on the device and hence this process is repeated if the user takes off and puts the device back on or if the device reboots or wakes up from sleep.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-721">当 uncalibrated 用户进入设备时，会有一些系统行为随 "自动目视定位" 功能发生变化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-721">There are a few system behavior changes with Auto Eye Position feature when an uncalibrated user puts on the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-722">在这种情况下，uncalibrated 用户指的是先前尚未经历设备上的目视跟踪校准过程的人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-722">In this context, an uncalibrated user refers to someone who has not gone through the eye tracking calibration process on the device previously.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="c256e-723">活动应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-723">Active Application</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="c256e-724">之前的行为</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-724">Prior Behavior</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="c256e-725">Windows 全息版20H2 更新中的行为</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-725">Behavior from Windows Holographic, version 20H2 Update</span></span> |
|:-------------------|:-----------------|:-----------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="c256e-726">未启用注视的应用或全息 Shell</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-726">Non-gaze enabled app or Holographic Shell</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="c256e-727">显示 "目视跟踪校准提示" 对话框。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-727">Eye tracking calibration prompt dialog is displayed.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="c256e-728">不显示提示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-728">No prompt is displayed.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="c256e-729">已启用注视的应用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-729">Gaze enabled app</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="c256e-730">显示 "目视跟踪校准提示" 对话框。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-730">Eye tracking calibration prompt dialog is displayed.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="c256e-731">仅当应用程序访问眼睛注视流时才显示眼睛跟踪校准提示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-731">Eye tracking calibration prompt is displayed only when the application accesses eye gaze stream.</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-732">如果用户从未启动的已启用的应用程序转换到访问看不到的数据的应用程序，则将显示校准提示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-732">If the user transitions from a non-gaze enabled application to one that accesses the gaze data, the calibration prompt will be displayed.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-733">当当前用户没有活动的目视跟踪校准时，所有其他系统行为将类似于。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-733">All other system behavior will be similar to when the current user does not have an active eye tracking calibration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-734">例如，不会启用单手启动手势。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-734">For example, the One-handed Start gesture will not be enabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-735">初始设置时，不会更改"开箱即用体验"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-735">There will be no change to the Out-Of-Box-Experience for initial setup.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-736">对于需要眼睛凝视数据或非常精确的全息影像定位的体验，我们建议未校准的用户运行眼动跟踪校准。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-736">For experiences that require eye gaze data or very precise hologram positioning, we recommend uncalibrated users to run eye tracking calibration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-737">可以通过眼动跟踪校准提示或从开始菜单启动"设置"应用，然后选择"系统"">校准 **">""** 眼>校准"来访问它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-737">It is accessible from the eye tracking calibration prompt or by launching the Settings app from the start menu, and then selecting **System > Calibration > Eye Calibration > Run eye calibration**.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-738">稍后可与其他校准信息 [一起找到此信息](hololens-calibration.md#auto-eye-position-support)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-738">This information can be found later with [other calibration information](hololens-calibration.md#auto-eye-position-support).</span></span> 

### <a name="certificate-manager"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-739">证书管理器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-739">Certificate Manager</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-740">通过新的证书管理器改进了设备安全性和符合性的审核、诊断和验证工具。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-740">Improved auditing, diagnosis, and validation tooling for device security and compliance through the new Certificate Manager.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-741">此功能可让你在商业环境中大规模部署、排查和验证证书。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-741">This capability will enable you to deploy, troubleshoot, and validate your certificates at scale in commercial environments.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-742">在 Windows Holographic 版本 20H2 中，我们将在"设置"应用中添加HoloLens 2管理器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-742">In Windows Holographic version 20H2, we are adding a Certificate Manager in the HoloLens 2 Settings app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-743">转到"**设置>更新&安全>证书"。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-743">Go to **Settings > Update & Security > Certificates**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-744">此功能提供了一种简单且用户友好的方式来查看、安装和删除设备上证书。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-744">This feature provides a simple and user-friendly way to view, install and remove certificates on your device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-745">借助新的证书管理器，管理员和用户现在改进了审核、诊断和验证工具，以确保设备保持安全且合规。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-745">With the new Certificate Manager, admins and users now have improved auditing, diagnosis and validation tooling to ensure that devices remain secure and compliant.</span></span> 

-   <span data-ttu-id="c256e-746">**审核：** 能够验证证书是否正确部署，或确认证书已正确删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-746">**Auditing:** Ability to validate that a certificate is deployed correctly or to confirm that it was removed appropriately.</span></span> 
-   <span data-ttu-id="c256e-747">**诊断：** 出现问题时，验证设备上是否存在相应的证书可节省时间，并有助于进行故障排除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-747">**Diagnosis:** When issues arise, validating that the appropriate certificates exist on the device saves time and helps with troubleshooting.</span></span> 
-   <span data-ttu-id="c256e-748">**验证：** 验证证书是否符合预期目的且正常运行，可以节省大量时间，尤其是在商业环境中，然后再大规模部署证书。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-748">**Validation:** Verifying that a certificate serves the intended purpose and is functional, can save significant time, particularly in commercial environments before deploying certificates at larger scale.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-749">若要在列表中快速查找特定证书，有一些选项可以按名称、存储或到期日期进行排序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-749">To find a specific certificate in the list quickly, there are options to sort by name, store or expiration date.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-750">用户还可以直接搜索证书。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-750">Users may also directly search for a certificate.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-751">若要查看单个证书属性，请选择证书，然后单击"信息 **"。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-751">To view individual certificate properties, select the certificate and click on **Info**.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-752">证书安装当前支持 .cer 和 .crt 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-752">Certificate installation currently supports .cer and .crt files.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-753">设备所有者可以在本地计算机和当前用户中安装证书; 所有其他用户只能安装到当前用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-753">Device Owners can install certificates in Local Machine and Current User;  all other users can only install into Current User.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-754">用户只能删除直接从 "设置" UI 安装的证书。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-754">Users can only remove certificates installed directly from the Settings UI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-755">如果通过其他方式安装了证书，则该证书还必须通过相同的机制删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-755">If a certificate has been installed through other means, it must also be removed by the same mechanism.</span></span>

#### <a name="to-install-a-certificate"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-756">若要安装证书：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-756">To install a certificate:</span></span> 

1.  <span data-ttu-id="c256e-757">将 HoloLens 2 连接到 PC。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-757">Connect your HoloLens 2 to a PC.</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="c256e-758">将要安装的证书文件放在 HoloLens 2 上的某个位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-758">Place the certificate file you want to install in a location on your HoloLens 2.</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="c256e-759">导航到 " **设置" 应用 > 更新 & 安全 > 证书**，并选择 "安装证书"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-759">Navigate to **Settings App > Update & Security > Certificates**, and select Install a certificate.</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="c256e-760">单击 " **导入文件** "，并导航到保存证书的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-760">Click **Import File** and navigate to the location you saved the certificate.</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="c256e-761">选择 " **存储位置**"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-761">Select **Store Location**.</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="c256e-762">选择 " **证书存储**"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-762">Select **Certificate Store**.</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="c256e-763">单击“安装”  。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-763">Click **Install**.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-764">现在应在设备上安装证书。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-764">The certificate should now be installed on the device.</span></span>

#### <a name="to-remove-a-certificate"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-765">删除证书的步骤：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-765">To remove a certificate:</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-766">导航到 " **设置" 应用 > 更新和安全 > 证书**"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-766">Navigate to **Settings App > Update and Security > Certificates**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-767">在搜索框中按名称搜索证书。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-767">Search for the certificate by name in the search box.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-768">选择证书。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-768">Select the certificate.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-769">单击 "**删除**"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-769">Click **Remove**</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-770">出现确认提示时，选择“是”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-770">Select **Yes** when prompted for confirmation.</span></span>

!["设置" 应用中的证书查看器](images/certificate-viewer-device.jpg)

![显示如何使用证书 UI 安装证书的图片](images/certificate-device-install.jpg)

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-773">稍后可 [在新的证书管理器页中](certificate-manager.md)找到此信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-773">This information can be found later [on a new Certificate Manager page](certificate-manager.md).</span></span>

### <a name="auto-launch-provisioning-from-usb"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-774">从 USB 自动启动设置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-774">Auto-launch provisioning from USB</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-775">在 OOBE 期间使用带预配包的 USB 驱动器时，自动化过程允许较少的用户交互。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-775">Automated processes allowing for less user interaction, when USB Drives with Provisioning Packages are used during OOBE.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-776">在此版本之前，用户必须手动在 OOBE 期间启动预配屏幕，才能使用按钮组合进行预配。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-776">Before this release users had to launch the provisioning screen manually during OOBE to provision using a button combination.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-777">现在，用户可以通过使用 USB 存储驱动器上的预配包跳过按钮组合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-777">Now users can skip the button combination, by using a Provisioning Package on a USB storage drive.</span></span> 

1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-778">在 OOBE 的第一个可交互时刻使用预配包插入 USB 驱动器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-778">Plug in the USB drive with the provisioning package during OOBE’s first interactable moment</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-779">当设备准备好进行预配时，它会自动打开包含预配页的提示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-779">When the device is ready to be provisioned it will automatically open the prompt with the provisioning page.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-780">注意：如果在设备启动时 USB 驱动器已接通电源，则 OOBE 将枚举现有的 USB 存储设备，并监视插入的其他 USB 存储设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-780">Note: If a USB drive is left plugged in while the device is booting then OOBE will enumerate existing USB storage device, as well as watch for additional ones being plugged in.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-781">有关在 OOBE 期间应用预配包的信息，请访问 [HoloLens 预配](hololens-provisioning.md#apply-a-provisioning-package-to-hololens-during-setup) 文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-781">For more information about applying provisioning packages during OOBE, visit the [HoloLens provisioning](hololens-provisioning.md#apply-a-provisioning-package-to-hololens-during-setup) documentation.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-782">有关从 [USB 自动启动预配](hololens-provisioning.md#auto-launch-provisioning-from-usb) 的其他信息，请参阅 HoloLens 预配文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-782">Additional information on [auto-launch provisioning from a USB](hololens-provisioning.md#auto-launch-provisioning-from-usb) can be found in the HoloLens provisioning documentation.</span></span>

### <a name="auto-confirm-provisioning-packages-in-oobe"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-783">在 OOBE 中自动确认预配包</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-783">Auto-confirm provisioning packages in OOBE</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-784">自动化过程允许较少的用户交互，当显示"预配包"页时，它将自动应用列出的所有包。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-784">Automated process allowing for less user interaction, when the Provisioning Package page is displayed it will automatically apply all packages listed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-785">当预配主屏幕出现时，OOBE 将倒计时 10 秒，然后自动开始应用所有预配包。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-785">When the provisioning main screen comes up, OOBE will count down 10 seconds before automatically starting applying all provisioning packages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-786">在验证 [预期的包](hololens-provisioning.md#auto-confirm-provisioning-packages-in-oobe) 后，用户仍然可以在此 10 秒内确认或取消。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-786">Users can still [confirm or cancel](hololens-provisioning.md#auto-confirm-provisioning-packages-in-oobe) within this 10 seconds after verifying the packages they expected.</span></span>

### <a name="automatic-provisioning-without-using-ui"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-787">无需使用 UI 即可自动预配</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-787">Automatic provisioning without using UI</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-788">合并了自动过程，减少了预配的设备交互。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-788">Combined automatic processes for reduced device interactions for provisioning.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-789">通过将从 USB 设备自动启动预配和自动确认预配包相结合，用户可以自动预配 HoloLens 2 设备，而无需使用设备的 UI，甚至无需设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-789">By combining the auto-launch of provisioning from USB devices and the auto-confirmation of provisioning packages, a user can provision HoloLens 2 devices automatically without using the device's UI or even wearing the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-790">你可以继续为多个设备使用相同的 USB 驱动器和预配包。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-790">You may continue to use the same USB drive and provisioning package for multiple devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-791">这可用于在同一区域中一次部署多个设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-791">This is useful for deploying multiple devices at once in the same area.</span></span> 

1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-792">使用[Windows 配置设计器](https://www.microsoft.com/store/productId/9NBLGGH4TX22)[创建预配包](hololens-provisioning.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-792">[Create a Provisioning Package](hololens-provisioning.md) using [Windows Configuration Designer](https://www.microsoft.com/store/productId/9NBLGGH4TX22).</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-793">将包复制到 USB 存储驱动器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-793">Copy the package to a USB storage drive.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-794">将[HoloLens 2 刷新](hololens-insider.md#ffu-download-and-flash-directions)到[19041.1361 或更高版本](https://aka.ms/hololens2previewdownload)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-794">[Flash your HoloLens 2](hololens-insider.md#ffu-download-and-flash-directions) to [19041.1361 or newer build](https://aka.ms/hololens2previewdownload).</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-795">当 [高级恢复助理](https://www.microsoft.com/store/productId/9P74Z35SFRS8) 已完成时，设备将拔出 USB-C 电缆。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-795">When [Advanced Recovery Companion](https://www.microsoft.com/store/productId/9P74Z35SFRS8) has completed flashing your device unplug your USB-C cable.</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-796">将 u 盘插入设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-796">Plug in your USB drive to the device.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-797">当 HoloLens 2 设备启动到 OOBE 时，它会自动检测 USB 驱动器上的预配包，并启动设置页面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-797">When the HoloLens 2 device boots into OOBE it will automatically detect the provisioning package on the USB drive and launch the provisioning page.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-798">10秒后，设备会自动应用预配包。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-798">After 10 seconds the device will automatically apply the provisioning package.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-799">你的设备现在已配置，并将 [显示设置成功屏幕](hololens-provisioning.md#automatic-provisioning-without-using-ui)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-799">Your device is now configured and will [display the Provisioning Successful screen](hololens-provisioning.md#automatic-provisioning-without-using-ui).</span></span>

### <a name="using-autopilot-with-wi-fi-connection"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-800">将 Autopilot 与 Wi-Fi 连接结合使用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-800">Using Autopilot with Wi-Fi connection</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-801">通过使 Autopilot 能够在 Wi-Fi 连接的设备上正常工作，已消除了将 USB C 适配器连接到以太网以降低硬件需求的需要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-801">Removed need for USB-C adapters to ethernet reducing hardware needs, by enabling Autopilot to function on Wi-Fi connected devices.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-802">现在，在 OOBE 期间，一旦使用 Wi-fi 连接了 HoloLens 2，OOBE 就会检查设备的 Autopilot 配置文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-802">Now during OOBE, once you connect HoloLens 2 with Wi-Fi, OOBE will check for an Autopilot profile for the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-803">如果找到一个，它将用于完成 AAD 联接和注册流的其余部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-803">If one is found it will be used to complete rest of the AAD join and enrollment flow.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-804">换句话说，不再需要使用以太网到 USB-C 或 Wi-Fi 到 USB-C 适配器，因为在 OOBE 开始时提供了它们。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-804">In other words, using ethernet to USB-C or Wi-Fi to USB-C adapter is not a requirement anymore, however they continue to work if provided at beginning of OOBE.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-805">详细了解 [适用于 HoloLens 2 设备的 Autopilot](hololens2-autopilot.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-805">Learn more about [Autopilot for HoloLens 2 devices](hololens2-autopilot.md).</span></span>

### <a name="tenantlockdown-csp-and-autopilot"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-806">Tenantlockdown CSP 和 Autopilot</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-806">Tenantlockdown CSP and Autopilot</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-807">通过设备重置或刷新将设备锁定到租户，从而使其在组织的租户上保持不变。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-807">Keeps devices on the organization's tenant by locking them to the tenant even through device reset or reflash.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-808">通过设置，禁止在中创建帐户，从而增强安全性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-808">With further security by disallowing account creation in via provisioning.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-809">HoloLens 2 设备现在支持 TenantLockdown CSP，如 [Windows 全息版 20H2](hololens-release-notes.md#windows-holographic-version-20h2)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-809">HoloLens 2 devices now support TenantLockdown CSP as of [Windows Holographic version 20H2](hololens-release-notes.md#windows-holographic-version-20h2).</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-810">[TenantLockdown](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/tenantlockdown-csp) CSP 使 HoloLens 2 仅限使用 Autopilot 绑定到 MDM 注册。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-810">[TenantLockdown](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/tenantlockdown-csp) CSP enables HoloLens 2 to be tied to MDM enrollment using Autopilot only.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-811">将 TenantLockdown CSP 的 RequireNetworkInOOBE 节点设置为 true 或 false 后 (初始在 HoloLens 2 上设置) 值，即使重新闪烁、OS 更新等，该值仍保留在设备上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-811">Once TenantLockdown CSP’s RequireNetworkInOOBE node is set to either true or false (initially set) value on HoloLens 2, that value remains on the device despite re-flashing, OS updates, etc.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-812">在 HoloLens 2 上将 TenantLockdown CSP 的 RequireNetworkInOOBE 节点设置为 true 后，OOBE 将无限期等待 Autopilot 配置文件在网络连接后成功下载并应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-812">Once TenantLockdown CSPs’ RequireNetworkInOOBE node is set to true on HoloLens 2, OOBE waits indefinitely for Autopilot profile to be successfully downloaded and applied, after network connectivity.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-813">当 TenantLockdown CSP 的 RequireNetworkInOOBE 节点在 HoloLens 2 设置为 true 后，OOBE 中将禁止以下操作：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-813">Once TenantLockdown CSPs’ RequireNetworkInOOBE node is set to true on HoloLens 2, following operations are disallowed in OOBE:</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-814">使用运行时预配创建本地用户</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-814">Creating local user using runtime provisioning</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-815">通过Azure AD执行联接操作</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-815">Performing Azure AD join operation via runtime provisioning</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-816">选择在 OOBE 体验中拥有设备的人</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-816">Selecting who owns the device in OOBE experience</span></span> 

#### <a name="how-to-set-this-using-intune"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-817">如何使用 Intune 设置此设置？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-817">How to set this using Intune?</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-818">创建自定义 OMA URI 设备配置文件，并指定 RequireNetworkInOOBE 节点的 true，如下所示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-818">Create a custom OMA URI device configuration profile and specify true for RequireNetworkInOOBE node as shown below.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="c256e-819">OMA-URI 值应为 ./Vendor/MSFT/TenantLockdown/RequireNetworkInOOBE</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-819">OMA-URI value should be ./Vendor/MSFT/TenantLockdown/RequireNetworkInOOBE</span></span>

   > [!div class="mx-imgBorder"]
   > <span data-ttu-id="c256e-820">![通过 OMA-URI 设置锁定](images/hololens-tenant-lockdown.png)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-820">![Setting tennant lockdown via OMA-URI](images/hololens-tenant-lockdown.png)</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-821">创建一个组，并将设备配置文件分配给该设备组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-821">Create a group and assign the device configuration profile to that device group.</span></span> 

1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-822">使HoloLens 2在上一步中创建的组的设备成员，并触发同步。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-822">Make the HoloLens 2 device member of the group created in previous step and trigger sync.</span></span>  

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-823">在 Intune 门户中验证设备配置是否已成功应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-823">Verify in the Intune portal that device configuration has been successfully applied.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-824">此设备配置成功应用于 HoloLens 2后，TenantLockdown 的效果将处于活动状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-824">Once this device configuration successfully applies on the HoloLens 2 device, effects of TenantLockdown will be active.</span></span>

#### <a name="how-to-unset-tenantlockdowns-requirenetworkinoobe-on-hololens-2-using-intune"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-825">如何使用 Intune 在 HoloLens 2上取消设置 TenantLockdown 的 RequireNetworkInOOBE？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-825">How to unset TenantLockdown’s RequireNetworkInOOBE on HoloLens 2 using Intune?</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-826">从HoloLens 2之前为其分配了设备配置的设备组中删除该配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-826">Remove the HoloLens 2 from the device group to which the device configuration created above was previously assigned.</span></span> 

1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-827">创建自定义基于 OMA URI 的设备配置文件，并指定 RequireNetworkInOOBE 的 false，如下所示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-827">Create a custom OMA URI based device configuration profile and specify false for RequireNetworkInOOBE as shown below.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-828">OMA-URI 值应为 ./Vendor/MSFT/TenantLockdown/RequireNetworkInOOBE</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-828">OMA-URI value should be ./Vendor/MSFT/TenantLockdown/RequireNetworkInOOBE</span></span>

   > [!div class="mx-imgBorder"]
   > <span data-ttu-id="c256e-829">![通过 Intune 中的 OMA URI 将 RequireNetworkInOOBE 设置为 false 的屏幕截图](images/hololens-tenant-lockdown-false.png)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-829">![Screenshot of setting RequireNetworkInOOBE to false via OMA URI in Intune](images/hololens-tenant-lockdown-false.png)</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-830">创建一个组，并将设备配置文件分配给该设备组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-830">Create a group and assign the device configuration profile to that device group.</span></span> 

1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-831">使HoloLens 2在上一步中创建的组的设备成员，并触发同步。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-831">Make the HoloLens 2 device member of the group created in previous step and trigger sync.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-832">在 Intune 门户中验证是否已成功应用设备配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-832">Verify in the Intune portal that device configuration has been successfully applied.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-833">此设备配置成功应用于 HoloLens 2 设备后，TenantLockdown 的效果将处于非活动状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-833">Once this device configuration successfully applies on the HoloLens 2 device, effects of TenantLockdown will be inactive.</span></span> 

#### <a name="what-would-happen-during-oobe-if-autopilot-profile-is-unassigned-on-a-hololens-after-tenantlockdown-was-set-to-true"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-834">如果 TenantLockdown 设置为 true 后在 HoloLens 上未分配 Autopilot 配置文件，则在 OOBE 期间将发生什么情况？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-834">What would happen during OOBE, if Autopilot profile is unassigned on a HoloLens after TenantLockdown was set to true?</span></span> 
<span data-ttu-id="c256e-835">OOBE 会无限期等待 Autopilot 配置文件下载并显示以下对话框。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-835">OOBE will wait indefinitely for Autopilot profile to download and following dialog will be presented.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-836">若要删除 TenantLockdown 的效果，必须首先使用 Autopilot 向设备注册其原始租户，并且必须按照上一步骤中所述取消设置 TenantLockdown CSP 引入的限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-836">In order to remove effects of TenantLockdown, device must be enrolled with its original tenant first using Autopilot only and RequireNetworkInOOBE must be unset as described in previous step before restrictions introduced by TenantLockdown CSP are removed.</span></span> 

![设备上强制实施策略的设备内视图。](images/hololens-autopilot-lockdown.png)

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-838">此信息现在可在 [TENANTLOCKDOWN CSP 和 Autopilot](hololens2-autopilot.md#tenantlockdown-csp-and-autopilot)下的 Autopilot 的其余部分找到。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-838">This information can now be found alongside the rest of Autopilot under [Tenantlockdown CSP and Autopilot](hololens2-autopilot.md#tenantlockdown-csp-and-autopilot).</span></span>

### <a name="global-assigned-access--kiosk-mode"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-839">全局分配的访问–展台模式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-839">Global Assigned Access – Kiosk Mode</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-840">通过启用在系统级别应用展台模式的新展台方法，降低了展台的标识管理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-840">Reduced Identity management for Kiosk, by enabling new Kiosk method that applies Kiosk mode at the system level.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-841">这项新功能可让 IT 管理员为多个 app 展台模式（在系统级上适用）配置一个 HoloLens 2 设备，该模式与系统上的任何标识都无关联，并且适用于登录到该设备的所有用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-841">This new feature allows an IT Admin to configure a HoloLens 2 device for multiple app kiosk mode which is applicable at system level, has no affinity with any identity on the system and applies to everyone who signs into the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-842">有关此新功能的详细信息，请参阅 [HoloLens 全局分配的访问展台](hololens-global-assigned-access-kiosk.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-842">Read about this new feature in detail in the [HoloLens global assigned access kiosk](hololens-global-assigned-access-kiosk.md).</span></span>

### <a name="automatic-launch-of-an-application-in-multiple-app-kiosk-mode"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-843">在多应用展台模式下自动启动应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-843">Automatic launch of an application in multiple-app kiosk mode</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-844">自动应用启动的聚焦体验，进一步增加了为展台模式体验选择的 UI 和应用选择。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-844">Focused experience with automatic app launch, further increasing the UI and app selections chosen for Kiosk mode experiences.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-845">仅适用于多应用展台模式，并且只有1个应用可以使用下面的突出显示属性指定为自动启动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-845">Applies only to multiple-app kiosk mode and only 1 app can be designated to auto-launch using highlighted attribute below in Assigned Access configuration.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-846">当用户登录时，应用程序将自动启动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-846">Application is automatically launched when user signs-in.</span></span>

<AllowedApps>

### <a name="kiosk-mode-behavior-changes-for-handling-of-failures"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-847">用于处理故障的展台模式行为更改</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-847">Kiosk mode behavior changes for handling of failures</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-848">通过消除展台模式故障中的可用应用，更安全的展台模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-848">More secure Kiosk mode by eliminating available apps on Kiosk mode failures.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-849">早于在应用展台模式时遇到故障，HoloLens 用于显示 "开始" 菜单中的所有应用程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-849">Earlier on encountering failures in applying kiosk mode, HoloLens used to show up all applications in start menu.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-850">现在，在 Windows Holographic 版本 20H2 中，如果出现故障，开始菜单中不会显示任何应用，如下所示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-850">Now in Windows Holographic version 20H2 in the case of failures no apps will be shown in the start menu as below:</span></span> 

![当展台模式发生故障时，其外观的图像。](images/hololens-kiosk-failure-behavior.png )

### <a name="hololens-policies"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-852">HoloLens 策略</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-852">HoloLens Policies</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-853">专为 HoloLens 创建的用于管理设备的设备管理选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-853">Device management options specifically for HoloLens created for managing the device.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-854">为 Windows Holographic 版本 20H2 上的HoloLens 2设备创建了新的混合现实策略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-854">New mixed reality policies have been created for HoloLens 2 devices on Windows Holographic version 20H2.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-855">新的可控制设置包括：设置亮度、设置音量、禁用混合现实捕获中的音频录制、设置收集诊断的时间和 AAD 组成员身份缓存。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-855">New controllable settings include: setting brightness, setting volume, disabling audio recording in mixed reality captures, setting when diagnostics can be collected, and AAD group membership cache.</span></span>

### <a name="cache-azure-ad-group-membership-for-offline-kiosk"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-876">缓存 Azure AD 脱机展台的组成员身份</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-876">Cache Azure AD Group membership for offline Kiosk</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-877">已启用将脱机展台用于 AAD 组，最多60天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-877">Enabled Offline Kiosks to be used with AAD groups for up to 60 days.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-878">此策略控制允许使用 Azure AD 组成员身份缓存来指定已登录用户 Azure AD 组的指定访问配置的天数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-878">This policy controls for how many days, Azure AD group membership cache is allowed to be used for Assigned Access configurations targeting Azure AD groups for signed in user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-879">一旦将此策略值设置为大于0的值，则不使用缓存。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-879">Once this policy value is set to value greater than 0 only then cache is used otherwise not.</span></span>  

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-880">名称： AADGroupMembershipCacheValidityInDays URI 值：./Vendor/MSFT/Policy/Config/MixedReality/AADGroupMembershipCacheValidityInDays</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-880">Name: AADGroupMembershipCacheValidityInDays URI value: ./Vendor/MSFT/Policy/Config/MixedReality/AADGroupMembershipCacheValidityInDays</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-881">最小值为0天</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-881">Min - 0 days</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="c256e-882">最大-60 天</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-882">Max - 60 days</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-883">正确使用此策略的步骤：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-883">Steps to use this policy correctly:</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-884">为展台 Azure AD 组创建设备配置文件，并将其分配给 HoloLens 设备 (s) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-884">Create a device configuration profile for kiosk targeting Azure AD groups and assign it to HoloLens device(s).</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-885">创建基于自定义 OMA URI 的设备配置，该配置将此策略值设置为所需的天数 (> 0) 并将其分配给 HoloLens 设备 () 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-885">Create a custom OMA URI based device configuration which sets this policy value to desired number of days (> 0) and assign it to HoloLens device(s).</span></span> 
    1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-886">应在 OMA-URI 文本框中输入 URI 值作为/Vendor/MSFT/Policy/Config/MixedReality/AADGroupMembershipCacheValidityInDays。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-886">The URI value should be entered in OMA-URI text box as ./Vendor/MSFT/Policy/Config/MixedReality/AADGroupMembershipCacheValidityInDays</span></span>
    1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-887">该值可以介于最小值/最大允许值之间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-887">The value can be between min / max allowed.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-888">注册 HoloLens 设备，并验证这两项配置是否适用于设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-888">Enroll HoloLens devices and verify both configurations get applied to the device.</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-889">当 internet 可用时，让 Azure AD 用户1登录，一旦用户登录并 Azure AD 组成员身份已成功确认，就会创建缓存。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-889">Let Azure AD user 1 sign-in when internet is available, once user signs-in and Azure AD group membership is confirmed successfully, cache will be created.</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-890">现在 Azure AD 用户1可以使 HoloLens 脱机并将其用于展台模式，只要策略值允许 X 天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-890">Now Azure AD user 1 can take HoloLens offline and use it for kiosk mode as long as policy value allows for X number of days.</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-891">对于任何其他 Azure AD 用户 N，可以重复执行步骤4和步骤5。以下是任何 Azure AD 用户都必须使用 Internet 登录设备，因此至少可以确定它们是展台配置所针对的 Azure AD 组的成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-891">Steps 4 and 5 can be repeated for any other Azure AD user N. Key point here is that any Azure AD user must sign-in to device using Internet so at least once we can determine that they are member of Azure AD group to which Kiosk configuration is targeted.</span></span> 
 
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-892">直到 Azure AD 执行步骤4后，才会在 "断开连接" 环境中遇到失败行为。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-892">Until step 4 is performed for a Azure AD user will experience failure behavior mentioned in “disconnected” environments.</span></span> 

### <a name="new-device-restriction-policies-for-hololens-2"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-893">HoloLens 2 的新设备限制策略</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-893">New device restriction policies for HoloLens 2</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-894">允许用户管理特定的设备管理策略，例如阻止添加或删除预配包。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-894">Allows users to manage specific device management policies such as blocking adding or removing provisioning packages.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-895">新启用的策略，允许对设备HoloLens 2选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-895">Newly enabled policies that allow for more management options of HoloLens 2 devices.</span></span> 
- [<span data-ttu-id="c256e-896">AllowAddProvisioningPackage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-896">AllowAddProvisioningPackage</span></span>](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/policy-csp-security#security-allowaddprovisioningpackage)

### <a name="research-mode"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-940">研究模式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-940">Research mode</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="c256e-941">在研究模式下，HoloLens 2成为计算机视觉研究的重要工具。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-941">While in Research Mode, the HoloLens 2 becomes a potent tool for computer vision research.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-942">与以前的版本相比，HoloLens 2研究模式具有以下优点：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-942">Compared to previous editions, Research Mode for HoloLens 2 has the following advantages:</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="c256e-943">除了在 HoloLens (第一代) 研究模式下公开的传感器外，我们现在提供 IMU 传感器访问，包括加速计、陀螺仪和磁力计。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-943">In addition to sensors exposed in HoloLens (1st gen) Research Mode, we now provide IMU sensor access including an accelerometer, gyroscope, and magnetometer.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="c256e-944">HoloLens 2提供了可以与研究模式一起使用的新功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-944">HoloLens 2 provides new capabilities that can be used together with Research Mode.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-945">具体而言，可以访问可交付更丰富试验集的表达式手部跟踪和眼动跟踪 API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-945">Specifically, access to articulated hand-tracking and eye-tracking APIs that can deliver a richer set of experiments.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-946">研究人员现在可以选择在 HoloLens 设备上启用研究模式，以访问所有这些面向外部的原始图像传感器流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-946">Researchers now have the option of enabling Research Mode on their HoloLens devices to access all of these external facing raw image sensors streams.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-947">研究模式HoloLens 2提供对加速计、陀螺仪和磁力计读数的访问。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-947">Research Mode for HoloLens 2 also provides access to the accelerometer, gyroscope, and magnetometer readings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-948">为了保护用户的隐私，无法通过研究模式使用原始眼动跟踪相机图像，但可以通过现有 API 获得眼睛凝视方向。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-948">To protect users’ privacy, raw eye-tracking camera images are not available through Research Mode, but eye-gaze direction  is available through existing APIs.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-949">有关更多 [技术详细信息，请查看](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/research-mode) 研究模式文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-949">Check out the [Research Mode documentation](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/research-mode) for further technical details.</span></span>

### <a name="recording-length-increased"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-950">录制长度增加</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-950">Recording length increased</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="c256e-951">根据客户反馈，我们增加了混合现实捕获 [的录制长度](holographic-photos-and-videos.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-951">Due to customer feedback we’ve increased the recording length of [mixed reality captures](holographic-photos-and-videos.md).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-952">默认情况下，混合现实捕获将不再限制为 5 分钟，而是根据可用磁盘空间计算最大录制长度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-952">Mixed reality captures will no longer be limited to 5 minutes by default but instead will calculate the maximum recording length based on available disk space.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-953">设备将基于可用磁盘空间估计最大视频录制持续时间，最多占总磁盘空间的 80%。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-953">The device will estimate the max video recording duration based on available disk space up to 80% of the total disk space.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-954">如果发生下列情况之一 (HoloLens) 5 分钟：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-954">The HoloLens will use default video recording length (5 minutes) if one of the following occurs:</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="c256e-955">估计的最大录制持续时间小于默认的 5 分钟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-955">The estimated max recording duration is smaller than the default 5 mins.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="c256e-956">可用磁盘空间小于总磁盘空间的 20%。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-956">The available disk space is less than 20% of the total disk space.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-957">可以在全息照片和视频文档中 [找到完整](holographic-photos-and-videos.md#maximum-recording-length) 要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-957">You can find the full requirements in our [holographic photos and videos](holographic-photos-and-videos.md#maximum-recording-length) documentation.</span></span> 

### <a name="improvements-and-fixes-in-the-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-958">更新中的改进和修复：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-958">Improvements and fixes in the update:</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-959">OOBE 中的更多屏幕现在以深色模式显示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-959">More screens in OOBE  are now in dark mode.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-960">了解更多内容应联机指向最新的隐私声明。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-960">Learn more content should point to the latest Privacy Statement online.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-961">解决了用户无法通过设置包预配 VPN 配置文件的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-961">Addressed an issue where users could not provision VPN profiles through provisioning packages.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-962">修复了 VPN 连接的代理配置问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-962">Fixed proxy configuration issue for VPN connection.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-963">已更新策略以禁用通过 MDM for NCM for AllowUsbConnection 的 USB 函数的枚举。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-963">Updated policy to disable enumeration of USB functions through MDM for NCM for AllowUsbConnection.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-964">解决了在将设备设置为 [单应用展台](hololens-kiosk.md)时，会阻止 HoloLens 设备在文件资源管理器中显示在文件资源管理器中的问题， (MTP) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-964">Addressed an issue that prevented a HoloLens device from showing up in File Explorer over Media Transfer Protocol (MTP) when the device is set up as a [single-app kiosk](hololens-kiosk.md).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-965">请注意，一般) 中的 MTP (和 USB 连接仍可使用 [AllowUSBConnection](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/policy-csp-connectivity#connectivity-allowusbconnection) 策略进行禁用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-965">Note that MTP (and USB connection in general) can still be disabled using the [AllowUSBConnection](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/policy-csp-connectivity#connectivity-allowusbconnection) policy.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-966">修复了 "开始" 菜单中的图标在展台模式下正确缩放的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-966">Fixed an issue where icons in the Start menu were scaled correctly in Kiosk mode.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-967">修复了由于 HTTP 缓存干扰以展台模式为目标 Azure AD 组的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-967">Fixed an issue due to HTTP caching interfering with kiosk mode targeted to Azure AD groups.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-968">修复了在使用预配包启用开发人员模式后，用户无法使用 "取消" 按钮的问题，除非他们禁用并重新启用了开发人员模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-968">Fixed an issue where users were unable to use the Pair button after enabling Developer mode with provisioning packages unless they disabled and re-enabled Developer mode.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-2004---september-2020-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-979">Windows 全息，版本 2004-2020 更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-979">Windows Holographic, version 2004 - September 2020 Update</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-980">内部版本 19041.1117</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-980">Build 19041.1117</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-981">更新中的改进和修复：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-981">Improvements and fixes in the update:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-982">解决了当 appxmanifest Visual Studio SupportsMultipleInstances="true"时阻止用户调试应用程序的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-982">Addresses an issue that prevented Visual Studio from debugging an application when SupportsMultipleInstances=”true” is present in the appxmanifest.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-983">此版本包括 NCSI 代理检测修补程序，用于解决通过网络代理进行 Internet 检测失败的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-983">This release includes NCSI proxy detection fix to address failed Internet detection over network proxy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-984">NCSI 可以使用计算机代理和按配置文件代理进行 Internet 连接检测。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-984">NCSI can use machine proxy and per-profile proxy for Internet connectivity detection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-985">NCSI 将在未来版本中支持每用户代理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-985">Per-user proxy will be supported by NCSI in future release.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-986">在大多数Windows Mixed Reality，当用户的头部处于向前的中性位置时，向前向向量与地面并行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-986">On most Windows Mixed Reality devices, the forward direction vector is parallel to the ground when the user's head is in a neutral position looking forward.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-987">但是，早期版本的 HoloLens 2使矢量与显示面板垂直，而显示面板相对于理想方向向下倾斜几度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-987">However, earlier versions of HoloLens 2 aligned the vector to be perpendicular to the display panels instead, which is tilted downward a few degrees relative to the ideal orientation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-988">较新版本的 HoloLens 2更正了此错误，以确保窗体因素之间的语义一致性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-988">Newer versions of HoloLens 2 have corrected this to ensure semantic consistency across form factors.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-989">改进了手部跟踪可靠度，这导致特定方案中的跟踪损失减少。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-989">Improved hand tracking robustness that will result in fewer tracking losses in specific scenarios.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-990">此版本包含一个修补程序，用于提高音频时间戳质量，这可能会导致视频捕获问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-990">This release contains a fix to improve audio timestamp quality which may have contributed to video capture issues.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1032">改进了录制视频中的全息影像稳定性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1032">Improved hologram stability in recorded videos.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1033">解决了混合现实捕获在设备处于待机状态多天后无法录制视频的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1033">Resolved an issue where mixed reality capture couldn't record video after the device was left in standby state for multiple days.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1034">对于 Unity 应用程序，通常禁用 HolographicSpace.UserPresence API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1034">The HolographicSpace.UserPresence API is generally disabled for Unity applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1035">此行为可避免在视器翻转时导致某些应用暂停的问题，即使启用了"在后台运行"设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1035">This behavior avoids an issue that caused some apps to pause when the visor was flipped up, even if the "run in the background" setting was enabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1036">现已为 Unity 版本 2018.4.18 及更高版本以及 2019.3.4 及更高版本启用 API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1036">The API is now enabled for Unity versions 2018.4.18 and later and 2019.3.4 and later.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1037">通过证书设备门户访问Wi-Fi，Web 浏览器可能会由于证书无效而阻止对 的访问。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1037">When you access Device Portal over a Wi-Fi connection, a web browser might prevent access to due to an invalid certificate.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1038">即使设备证书以前受信任，浏览器也可能报告"ERR_SSL_PROTOCOL_ERROR"等错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1038">The browser might report an error such as "ERR_SSL_PROTOCOL_ERROR," even if the device certificate was previously trusted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1039">在这种情况下，无法继续设备门户，因为无法忽略安全警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1039">In this case, you can't progress to Device Portal, as there's no option to ignore security warnings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1040">此更新解决了问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1040">This update resolved the issue.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1041">如果先前已在电脑上下载并信任设备证书以删除浏览器安全警告，并且发生 SSL 错误，则必须下载新证书并将其信任，以解决浏览器安全警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1041">If the device certificate was previously downloaded and trusted on a PC to remove browser security warnings, and the SSL error occurs, the new certificate has to be downloaded and trusted to address browser security warnings.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1042">支持创建可通过使用 .MSIX 包安装应用的运行时预配包。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1042">Enabled the ability to create a runtime provisioning package that can install an app by using MSIX packages.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1043">添加了 **设置**  >  **系统**  >  **全息影像** 中的设置，该设置允许用户在设备关闭时自动删除混合现实主页中的所有全息影像。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1043">Added a setting in **Settings** > **System** > **Holograms** that allows users to automatically remove all holograms from Mixed Reality home when the device shuts down.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1044">修复了一个问题，该问题导致在 HoloLens 模拟器中将更改像素格式的 HoloLens 应用程序呈现为黑色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1044">Fixed an issue that caused HoloLens apps that change their pixel format to render black in the HoloLens emulator.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1045">修复了 Iris 登录期间导致崩溃的 bug。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1045">Fixed a bug that caused a crash during Iris login.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1046">修复了有关现有应用的重复存储下载的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1046">Fixed an issue about repeated store downloads for already-current apps.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1047">修复了一个 bug，以防止沉浸式应用重复打开 Microsoft Edge。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1047">Fixed a bug to prevent immersive apps from opening Microsoft Edge repeatedly.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1048">修复了从1903版更新后初始启动时启动照片应用的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1048">Fixed an issue with launches of the Photos app in initial boots after updating from the 1903 release.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1049">提高了性能和可靠性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1049">Improved performance and reliability.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-1903---june-2020-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-1050">Windows 全息，版本 1903-2020 更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1050">Windows Holographic, version 1903 - June 2020 Update</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1051">生成18362.1064</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1051">Build 18362.1064</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-1052">更新中的改进和修复：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1052">Improvements and fixes in the update:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1053">如果未指定自定义的 MRC 录像机，则为某些属性提供新的默认值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1053">Custom MRC recorders have new default values for certain properties if they aren't specified.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1054">在 *MRC 视频效果*：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1054">On the *MRC Video Effect*:</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1055">PreferredHologramPerspective (1 PhotoVideoCamera) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1055">PreferredHologramPerspective (1 PhotoVideoCamera)</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1056">GlobalOpacityCoefficient (0.9 (HoloLens) 1.0 (沉浸式耳机) ) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1056">GlobalOpacityCoefficient (0.9 (HoloLens) 1.0 (Immersive headset))</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1057">在 " *MRC 音频" 效果* 上：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1057">On the *MRC Audio Effect*:</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1058">LoopbackGain (Windows 设备门户中混合现实捕获页面上当前的 "应用音频增益" 值) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1058">LoopbackGain (the current "App Audio Gain" value on the Mixed Reality Capture page in Windows Device Portal)</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1059">MicrophoneGain (Windows 设备门户中混合现实捕获页面上的当前 "Mic 音频增益" 值) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1059">MicrophoneGain (the current "Mic Audio Gain" value on the Mixed Reality Capture page in Windows Device Portal)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1060">对于 Unity 应用程序，通常禁用 HolographicSpace.UserPresence API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1060">The HolographicSpace.UserPresence API is generally disabled for Unity applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1061">此行为可避免在视器翻转时导致某些应用暂停的问题，即使启用了在后台运行的设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1061">This behavior avoids an issue that causes some apps to pause when the visor is flipped up, even if the setting to run in the background is enabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1062">现已为 Unity 版本 2018.4.18 及更高版本以及 2019.3.4 及更高版本启用 API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1062">The API is now enabled for Unity versions 2018.4.18 and later, and 2019.3.4 and later.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1063">修复了导致 HoloLens 应用更改其像素格式以在 HoloLens 仿真器中呈现黑色的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1063">Fixed an issue that caused HoloLens apps that change their pixel format to render black in the HoloLens Emulator.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1064">修复了从 1903 版本更新后在初始启动中启动照片应用的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1064">Fixed an issue about launches of the Photos app in initial boots after updating from the 1903 release.</span></span>
