### <a name="support-for-windows-autopilot"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-1091">支持 Windows Autopilot</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1091">Support for Windows Autopilot</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-1092">Windows Autopilot for HoloLens 2 允许设备销售渠道预先注册到 Intune 租户中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1092">Windows Autopilot for HoloLens 2 lets the device sales channel pre-enroll HoloLens into your Intune tenant.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1093">设备到达后，它们就可以自行部署为租户下的共享设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1093">When devices arrive, they’re ready to self-deploy as shared devices under your tenant.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1094">若要利用自部署，设备必须在安装过程中的第一个屏幕上通过使用 USB 到以太网连接到网络。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1094">To take advantage of self-deployment, the device must connect to a network during the first screen in setup by using a USB-C-to-Ethernet.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-1095">用户启动 Autopilot 自行部署过程后，此过程将完成以下步骤：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1095">After a user starts the Autopilot self-deploying process, the process completes the following steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1096">将设备加入到 Azure Active Directory (Azure AD) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1096">Join the device to Azure Active Directory (Azure AD).</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1097">使用 Azure AD 在 Microsoft Intune (或其他 MDM 服务) 中注册设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1097">Use Azure AD to enroll the device in Microsoft Intune (or another MDM service).</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1098">下载设备目标策略、证书和网络配置文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1098">Download the device-targeted policies, certificates, and networking profiles.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1099">设置设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1099">Provision the device.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1100">向用户显示登录屏幕。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1100">Present the sign-in screen to the user.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-1101">有关详细信息，请参阅 [Windows Autopilot For HoloLens 2 评估指南](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens2-autopilot)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1101">Learn more from the [Windows Autopilot for HoloLens 2 evaluation guide](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens2-autopilot).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-1102">*请联系你的帐户管理员立即加入 AutoPilot preview。即将开始交付 Autopilot 的设备。*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1102">*Contact your Account Manager to join the AutoPilot preview now. Autopilot-ready devices will begin shipping soon.*</span></span>

### <a name="fido2-security-key-support"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-1103">FIDO2 安全密钥支持</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1103">FIDO2 security key support</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-1104">某些用户在工作或学校环境中与他人共享 HoloLens 设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1104">Some users share a HoloLens device with others in a work or school environment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1105">因此，用户可以轻松地无需键入长用户名和密码，这一点很重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1105">So it's important that users can easily without typing long user names and passwords.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1106">使用 Fast Identity Online (FIDO) ， (Azure AD租户中的) 无需输入用户名或密码即可无缝登录到 HoloLens。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1106">Fast Identity Online (FIDO) lets anyone in your organization (Azure AD tenant) seamlessly sign-in to HoloLens without entering a user name or password.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-1107">FIDO2 安全密钥是基于标准的"不可加密"无密码身份验证方法，可以采用任何外形要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1107">FIDO2 security keys are an "unphishable" standards-based passwordless authentication method that can come in any form factor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1108">FIDO 是无密码身份验证的开放标准。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1108">FIDO is an open standard for passwordless authentication.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1109">它允许用户和组织在没有用户名或密码的情况下登录到其资源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1109">It allows users and organizations to sign in to their resources without a user name or password.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1110">而是使用内置于设备的外部安全密钥或平台密钥。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1110">Instead they use an external security key or a platform key built into a device.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-1111">若要开始，请参阅 [启用无密码安全密钥登录](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/authentication/howto-authentication-passwordless-security-key)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1111">To get started, see [Enable passwordless security key sign-in](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/authentication/howto-authentication-passwordless-security-key).</span></span>

### <a name="improved-mdm-enrollment-via-provisioning-package"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-1112">通过预配包改进了 MDM 注册</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1112">Improved MDM enrollment via provisioning package</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-1113">预配包允许通过配置文件而不是 HoloLens 开箱即用体验来设置 HoloLens 配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1113">Provisioning packages let you set HoloLens configuration through a config file rather than through the HoloLens out-of-box experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1114">以前，预配包必须复制到 HoloLens 内部内存中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1114">Previously, provisioning packages had to be copied onto the HoloLens internal memory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1115">现在，它们可以位于 USB 驱动器上，以便更轻松地在多个 HoloLens 设备上重复使用，并且你可以并行预配设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1115">Now they can be on a USB drive so they're easier to reuse on multiple HoloLens devices and you can provision devices in parallel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1116">预配包现在还支持在设备管理中注册字段，因此预配后无需手动设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1116">Provisioning packages now also support a field to enroll in device management so there's no manual setup after provisioning.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-1117">试试看：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1117">To try it out:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1118">将最新版本的 Windows 配置设计器从 Windows 应用商店下载到电脑上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1118">Download the latest version of the Windows Configuration Designer from the Windows store onto your PC.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1119">选择 **"预配 HoloLens 设备**  >  **预配HoloLens 2设备"。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1119">Select **Provision HoloLens Devices** > **Provision HoloLens 2 devices**.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1120">生成配置文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1120">Build your configuration profile.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1121">然后将创建的所有文件复制到 USB-C 存储设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1121">Then copy all files that were created to a USB-C storage device.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1122">将 USB-C 设备插入任何全新闪烁的 HoloLens。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1122">Plug the USB-C device into any freshly flashed HoloLens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1123">然后按 **音量关闭**  +  **电源** 按钮以应用预配包。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1123">Then press the **volume down** + **power** buttons to apply your provisioning package.</span></span>

### <a name="line-of-business-application-install-status"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-1124">业务线应用程序安装状态</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1124">Line-of-business application install status</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-1125">适用于业务线应用的 MDM 应用部署和管理对于 HoloLens 至关重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1125">MDM app deployment and management for line of business apps is critical to HoloLens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1126">管理员和用户需要查看应用安装状态以进行审核和诊断。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1126">Admins and users need to view app install status for auditing and diagnosis.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1127">在此版本中，我们在 **设置**  >  **帐户**  >  **访问工作或学校**  >  **单击你的帐户信息时添加了**  >  更多详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1127">In this release, we added more details in **Settings** > **Accounts** > **Access work or school** > **Click on your account** > **Info**.</span></span>

### <a name="additional-csps-and-policies"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-1128">其他 Csp 和策略</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1128">Additional CSPs and policies</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-1129">[ (CSP) 的配置服务提供程序](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/configuration-service-provider-reference?redirectedfrom=MSDN)是一个用于读取、设置、修改或删除设备上的配置设置的接口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1129">A [configuration service provider (CSP)](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/configuration-service-provider-reference?redirectedfrom=MSDN) is an interface to read, set, modify, or delete configuration settings on a device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1130">在此版本中，我们添加了对更多策略的支持，以提高管理员对已部署的 HoloLens 设备的控制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1130">In this release, we add support for more policies to increase the control administrators have over deployed HoloLens devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1131">有关 HoloLens 支持的 Csp 列表，请参阅 [NETWORKQOSPOLICY CSP](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/networkqospolicy-csp)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1131">For the list of CSPs supported by HoloLens, see [NetworkQoSPolicy CSP](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/networkqospolicy-csp).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-1132">本版本中的新主题：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1132">New in this release:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-1133">**策略云解决方案提供商**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1133">**Policy CSP**</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-1134">策略配置服务提供程序使企业能够在 Windows 设备上配置策略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1134">The Policy configuration service provider enables the enterprise to configure policies on Windows devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1135">在此版本中，我们为 HoloLens 添加了新策略，这里列出了这些策略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1135">In this release, we added new policies for HoloLens, which are listed here.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1136">若要了解详细信息，请参阅 [HoloLens 2 支持的策略 csp](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/policies-supported-by-hololens2)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1136">To learn more, see [Policy CSPs supported by HoloLens 2](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/policies-supported-by-hololens2).</span></span>  

- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1137">LetAppsAccessCamera_ForceAllowTheseApps</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1137">LetAppsAccessCamera_ForceAllowTheseApps</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-1148">**NetworkQoSPolicy 云解决方案提供商**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1148">**NetworkQoSPolicy CSP**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-1149">NetworkQoSPolicy 配置服务提供商使用 QoS 策略创建 (服务质量) 提供程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1149">The NetworkQoSPolicy configuration service provider creates network quality-of-service (QoS) policies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1150">QoS 策略根据一组匹配的条件对网络流量执行一组操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1150">A QoS policy performs a set of actions on network traffic based on a set of matching conditions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1151">有关详细信息，请参阅 [NetworkQoSPolicy CSP](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/networkqospolicy-csp)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1151">To learn more, see [NetworkQoSPolicy CSP](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/networkqospolicy-csp).</span></span>

### <a name="expanded-usb-ethernet-support-for-5glte-tethered-devices"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-1152">扩展了对 5G/LTS 网络设备的 USB 以太网支持</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1152">Expanded USB Ethernet support for 5G/LTE tethered devices</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-1153">添加了支持，使某些移动宽带设备（如 5G/Wi-Fi 手机和 Wi-Fi 热点）通过 USB HoloLens 2连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1153">Support was added to enable certain mobile broadband devices, such as 5G/LTE phones and Wi-Fi hotspots, when they're tethered to the HoloLens 2 via USB.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1154">这些设备现在在网络设置 **中显示为** 另一个以太网连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1154">These devices are now displayed in **network settings** as another Ethernet connection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1155"> (不支持需要外部驱动程序的移动宽带设备。) 此功能在 Wi-Fi 不可用且 Wi-Fi Tethering 性能不足时启用高带宽连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1155">(Mobile broadband devices that require an external driver aren't supported.) This functionality enables high-bandwidth connections when Wi-Fi is not available and Wi-Fi tethering isn't performant enough.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1156">若要详细了解支持的 USB 设备，请参阅 [连接到蓝牙和 USB-C 设备](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens-connect-devices)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1156">To learn more about supported USB devices, see [Connect to Bluetooth and USB-C devices](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens-connect-devices).</span></span>  

### <a name="hand-tracking-improvements"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-1157">手部跟踪改进</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1157">Hand tracking improvements</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-1158">此版本包括多项手动跟踪改进：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1158">This release includes several hand tracking improvements:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1159">**指向姿势稳定性：** 现在，当手指被手指遮挡时，系统可以抵御手指的滑动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1159">**Pointing pose stability:** The system now resists bending the index finger when it gets occluded by the palm.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1160">此更改提高了按下按钮、键入、滚动内容等时的准确性！</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1160">This change improves the accuracy when you push buttons, type, scroll content, and more!</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1161">**减少了意外的敲击：** 改进了对敲击手势的检测。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1161">**Reduced accidental air taps:** We improved detection of the air tap gesture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1162">现在，在多种常见情况下（例如，将手放在一边时）中的意外激活更少。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1162">There are now fewer accidental activations in several common scenarios, such as when you drop your hands to your sides.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1163">**用户交换机可靠性：** 现在，共享设备时，系统在更新手部大小时速度更快且更可靠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1163">**User switch reliability:** The system is now faster and more reliable at updating the hand size when you share a device.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1164">**减少手部窃取：** 改进了传感器视图超过两手的情况的处理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1164">**Reduced hand stealing:** We improved handling of cases where there are more than two hands in view of the sensors.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1165">如果多人在一起工作，现在跟踪手从用户"跳转"到场景中其他人手的可能性要低得多。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1165">If multiple people are working close together, there's now a much lower chance that the tracked hand will "jump" from the user to the hand of someone else in the scene.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1166">**系统可靠性：** 修复了在设备负载较高时导致手部跟踪停止工作的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1166">**System reliability:** Fixed an issue that caused hand tracking to stop working when the device is under high load.</span></span>

### <a name="dark-mode"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-1167">深色模式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1167">Dark mode</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-1168">许多 Windows 应用现在支持深色和浅色模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1168">Many Windows apps now support both dark and light modes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1169">HoloLens 2用户可以为支持两者的应用选择默认模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1169">HoloLens 2 users can choose the default mode for apps that support both.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1170">更新之后，默认应用模式为 "深色"，但你可以轻松地更改此设置：导航到 "**设置**" "  >  **系统**  >  **颜色**" "  >  **选择默认的应用模式**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1170">After the update, the default app mode is "dark," but you can easily change this setting: Navigate to **Settings** > **System** > **Colors** > **Choose your default app mode**.</span></span>

### <a name="cortana-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-1187">Cortana 更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1187">Cortana updates</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-1188">更新后的应用程序可与 Microsoft 365 集成，以帮助你在设备上进行更多的操作， (当前仅 US-English) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1188">The updated app integrates with Microsoft 365 to help you get more done across your devices (currently in US-English only).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1189">在 HoloLens 2 上，Cortana 不再支持某些特定于设备的命令，例如调整音量或重新启动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1189">On HoloLens 2, Cortana no longer supports certain device-specific commands, like adjusting volume or restarting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1190">新的系统语音命令现在支持这些选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1190">These options are now supported by the new system voice commands.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1191">在 [博客](https://blogs.windows.com/windowsexperience/2020/02/28/cortana-in-the-upcoming-windows-10-release-focused-on-your-productivity-with-enhanced-security-and-privacy/)中了解有关新 Cortana 应用的详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1191">Learn more about the new Cortana app in our [blog](https://blogs.windows.com/windowsexperience/2020/02/28/cortana-in-the-upcoming-windows-10-release-focused-on-your-productivity-with-enhanced-security-and-privacy/).</span></span>

### <a name="quality-improvements-and-fixes"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-1192">质量改进和修复</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1192">Quality improvements and fixes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-1193">更新中也有改进和修复：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1193">Improvements and fixes also in the update:</span></span>  
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1194">引入了活动的显示校准系统。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1194">Introduced an active display calibration system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1195">此功能可改善全息影像的稳定性和对齐方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1195">This feature improves the stability and alignment of holograms.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1196">当你从一侧到另一侧时，它们现在就会保持不变。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1196">They now stay in place when you move your head from side to side.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1197">修复了一个 bug，在这种情况下，Wi-Fi 流式传输到 HoloLens 会定期中断。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1197">Fixed a bug where Wi-Fi streaming to HoloLens got disrupted periodically.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1198">如果应用程序指示它需要低延迟流式处理，请通过调用 [SetSocketMediaStreamingMode 函数](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/win32/api/socketapi/nf-socketapi-setsocketmediastreamingmode)来实现修复。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1198">If an application indicates that it needs low latency streaming, implement the fix by calling the [SetSocketMediaStreamingMode function](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/win32/api/socketapi/nf-socketapi-setsocketmediastreamingmode).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1199">修复了在研究模式下流式传输期间发生的设备挂起。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1199">Fixed a device hang that occurred during streaming in research mode.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1200">修复了以下 bug：在某些情况下，恢复会话时不会在登录屏幕上显示正确的用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1200">Fixed a bug where in some cases the right user wouldn't be displayed on the sign-in screen when resuming a session.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1201">修复了用户无法通过"设置"导出 MDM 日志 **的问题**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1201">Fixed an issue where users couldn't export MDM logs through **Settings**.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1202">修复了以下问题：在开箱即用设置后立即进行眼动跟踪的准确性可能低于预期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1202">Fixed an issue where the accuracy of eye tracking immediately following out-of-box setup could be lower than expected.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1203">修复了在某些情况下眼动跟踪子系统无法初始化或执行校准的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1203">Fixed an issue where the eye tracking subsystem failed to initialize or perform calibration under certain conditions.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1204">修复了提示已校准用户进行眼部校准的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1204">Fixed an issue where eye calibration would be prompted for an already-calibrated user.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1205">修复了驱动程序在眼部校准期间崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1205">Fixed an issue where a driver would crash during eye calibration.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1206">修复了重复按下电源按钮可能导致 60 秒系统超时和 shell 崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1206">Fixed an issue where repeated power button presses could cause a 60-second system timeout and shell crash.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1207">改进了深度缓冲区的稳定性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1207">Improved stability for depth buffers.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1208">在" **共享** "按钮反馈中心以便用户可以更轻松地共享反馈。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1208">Added a **Share** button in the Feedback Hub so users can more easily share feedback.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1209">修复了 RoboRaid wan 未正确安装的 bug。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1209">Fixed a bug where RoboRaid wan't installed correctly.</span></span>

### <a name="known-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-1210">已知问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1210">Known issues</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1211">zh-CN 系统语言的问题阻止语音命令捕获混合现实或显示设备 IP 地址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1211">An issue with the zh-CN system language prevents voice commands from taking a mixed reality capture or displaying the device IP address.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1212">问题要求在启动设备后启动 Cortana 应用，以使用"你好 Cortana"语音激活。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1212">An issue requires you to launch the Cortana app after starting the device to use "Hey Cortana" voice activation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1213">如果从 18362 版本更新，则还可以在"启动"中看到以前版本的 Cortana 应用的第二个应用 **磁贴**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1213">If you updated from a 18362 build, you may also see a second app tile for the previous version of the Cortana app that no longer works in **Start**.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-1903---may-2020-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-1214">Windows Holographic 版本 1903 - 2020 年 5 月更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1214">Windows Holographic, version 1903 - May 2020 Update</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="c256e-1215">内部版本 18362.1061</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1215">Build 18362.1061</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c256e-1216">此每月质量更新不包含任何值得注意的更改，因为团队正在处理 Windows Holographic 版本 2004 May Update，如前文所述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1216">This monthly quality update doesn't contain any notable changes because the team was working on the Windows Holographic version 2004 May Update, as described earlier.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-1903---april-2020-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="c256e-1217">Windows Holographic 版本 1903 - 2020 年 4 月更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c256e-1217">Windows Holographic, version 1903 - April 2020 Update</span></span>
